et lieve le keur qui est endroit la mice, ou li coutes dou malaide vient devers senestre, et soit li elevations dont tu lieves le keur selonc la keur, selonc la longesce dou cors, et li cautere soient selonc la largesce dou cors.	and hold the heart which is located in the mouse, or the pains come from the left side, and make the elevation according to the heart, according to the length of the body, and the cautery according to the width of the body.
Aprés i boute les II ners enflamez tant que li keurs soit perciez de l’autre part, et puis trai fuers le cautere, et ensi en i avra IIII.	After that, burn the two edges until the heart is pierced on the other side, and then treat the cautery fiercely, and so there will be four.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize a tot le cautere a III ners.	And if you see that the cautery is completely burned at three edges.
Aprés le cure quant il a geteit porriture par lonc tens, et ce vaut mues que li autre des cures devant dites.	After treatment when the pus has drained for a long time, this is more effective than any of the other treatments mentioned before.
de ydropisie	Of hydropsis
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	Cautery is not effective against hydrops, except in the manner known as "asclytes".
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis;	When you treat it according to the methods we have described in detail, and your treatment does not benefit the patient, then you must perform four cauterizations around the wound, one on the stomach, one on the liver, one on the heart, two behind the back over the spine, and one on the anus.
et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	and the cauterizations should be close to the area of pain.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere;	After leaving the cauterization open for a long time to allow pus to drain, do not leave the patient's treatment after cauterization.
et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	and healing would be hastened, and the two parts would be joined together with God's help.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit;	The form of the cautery for the belly should be the needle that we have shown before.
et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	and that for the back should be olive-shaped, according to what is placed before.
de l’enfleure des piez	of the swelling of the stones
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire;	When the feet are swollen in the hydroptic patient and are filled with yellowish pus, you should cauterize on the back of the foot between the little toe and the ring finger.
et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	and hold your hand with the cautery without pain returning.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And do not press too deeply, so as to close the natural opening; thus the heat from the fire will penetrate the flesh according to this form:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire;	After that, make two cauterizations on each leg with the tip of the cutting knife;
et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe;	and let the cauterization be long, one on the inside of the knee joint and the other on the outside of the leg;
et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse;	and leave the cauterizations healing for a long time without touching them, so they heal well;
aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	After the treatment of the other treatments we have mentioned.
de la menoison	of the wound
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures;	When abdominal pain arises from cold and moisture, and the retaining and digestive virtues in the stomach and intestines are weakened, it cannot be cured by any means.
et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule;	and you see the patient in great distress with strong pain, so make a severe cautery on the stomach according to what he has spoken about before, or cautery of the stomach, at the cautery of the circuit.
et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	and I cauterize around the anus gently at every cautery, and carefully tie off the threads, and II cauterize on the thighs.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et I cautere sus chaicun yle, et II petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	And if you see the moisture abundant and the patient suffering, make a burn on the finger, and a burn on every part, and small burns on the gentle stomach, for the cure is beneficial when there is good aid.
de la cure des emorroydes	**On the Treatment of Hemorrhoids**
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres:	When hemorrhoids are either internal or external, and they have been present for a long time, consisting of corrupt cold and moist humors, their treatment is as we have said in detail, but cauterization does not help.
III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois;	On the spine of the back, that which is entirely soaked with blood, gradually and in a triangular manner, and one should cauterize from below the wound, two fingers deep.
et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile;	and if you think his stomach is cold, and the meat does not cook, and one sees swelling on the face, then one should great cauterize the stomach as it has been said before, and another on the liver, and another on every part with a hot iron.
et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	and let the fire cautery grow long.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After treatment, reset the shoulder as long as it is healed.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	from the fleshiness called "thelul
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit;	When you have finished all else, if the cautery seems too sharp, then take a hot iron and apply it thoroughly to that part.
et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort;	and hold it there until the cautery reaches the vein, from which the blood flows.
fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit;	do this once or twice, and if there is much heat, cauterize each as we have said.
aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez;	after the treatment of wounds until they are healed;
et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	and if you cauterize with a large cautery on the scalp, it will bring greater aid.
de plaie mal curee	From the poorly treated wound
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the patient cannot endure cutting or incising, which we will describe in its place, such a disease comes that it cannot be healed except by cautery.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	When no vein becomes fistulated, and there is swelling, putrefaction, and corrupt moisture, you must try all sorts of subtle remedies, and be sure to know at every stage how effective they are.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing;	After heating the cautery to a sharp point, insert it into the fistula according to the amount that has entered, and repeat the cauterization once or twice, or even three times, depending on the quantity required;
et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	and beware of burning the sensitive nerves and great veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans;	It goes to the core of the bladder and intestines, so be careful with these joints, and do not make fire wounds except on fleshy parts, and know that it is not always permanent.
aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement;	After treatment, keep the joint as healthy as possible, and if the joints are successfully healed and the materials removed for a long time, then know that the joint is completely healthy.
et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font;	and if the materials are not removed, know that the joint is weak and the bone is corrupted at its base.
et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	and thus, as one of these things we will tell in its place.
de la maladie des reins	Of kidney disease
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit;	When the pain of a fracture comes with heavy bleeding and does not allow a woman to bear it, then you should perform cauterization on the wound from both sides, using the cautery claw that we have previously mentioned.
et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	and we should cauterize it in the middle, if there are three cauterizations in a row, and this will bring greater help.
de la vessie	Of the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce;	When the bladder is soft and weak due to pain and moisture, preventing the patient from urinating, then perform cauterization on the outside part of the bladder, where the hairs begin to grow, both on the right and left side, making each cauterization about as long as a finger.
et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing;	and he makes a fire cautery on the back, where it is needed;
et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	and he applies the cautery as described above.
de la marris	Of the pain
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde;	When the weather is cold and moist, and does not allow for conception, and the flowers are ruined and their ends are delayed.
et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor:	and when they come, they cause great pain:
adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos;	then it is necessary to make three cauterizations around the anus, as we have said in the cautery of the bladder, and two fire cauterizations on the back.
et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	and so the cautery should be done, as we have said.
de la hainche	de la hainche" translates to "of the spine
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble;	When viscous moisture descends into the chest cavity and for this reason it becomes silent in its place, and the signs are that the affected leg appears longer than the other when measured together.
et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle;	and it is found that the vulnerable parts are in the lower region, so it is necessary to cauterize the patient on the chest cavity with a cautery resembling a circle, and mark around the lung with a sign as it returns, so that the chest remains within the circle.
et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	and if they are cauterized like those used to cauterize the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs;	If this cauterization is not present, perform three cauterizations with hot olive oil, and make sure the cauterization is just as effective as all the others.
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and heal it as long as it is healthy.
de la dolor de la hainche	of the pain of the back (or "hainche" as written)
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene:	When pain arises in the chest due to cold and moisture, and the patient is cured using methods we have described in detail, but the treatment is ineffective, and the illness persists, it is ancient.
adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	So it is necessary for you to cleanse the patient of bad humours from foul or other good-looking pills.
Aprés li fai cautere;	Afterwards, he performs cautery;
et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres:	and the method of cautery is according to two manners:
c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	that is to say, the use of burning medicines and fire cautery.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz:	Fire cautery is according to many manners, some of which are as follows:
que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire;	That you cauterize the wound of the spine with three triangular cauterizations according to this form, making them deep and wide, and there should be between each cauterization a distance as thick as two fingers, and they shall be olive-shaped.
aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	Cauterization should never be done in the middle of the spine's top, for that reason there are three according to this form.
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche;	And if you see that the cauterization affects the circle we have mentioned in the dislocation of the spine,
mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	but make it in such a way that the circle contains all the hair, and every part of the heart is burnt.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	And this is the method used in sciatica when the pain is confined to the spine and does not reach the thigh or leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc;	And if it extends to the thigh and leg, make two cauterizations on the side where the patient feels the most pain, and one cauterization above the ankle on the left side slightly.
et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur;	and it should be a cutting cauterization, burning the thickness of the heart.
et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	and if the patient feels that the pain extends to both feet or near the anus, cauterize there where he feels the pain three times or four, with a cautery called "point.
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus;	And if it happens again, do more;
et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	And if the pain is intense in the knee down to the thigh, perform a cauterization with a sharp or circular instrument, and be very careful in all your cauterizations that you do not leave them too long so as not to burn the skin and large arteries, and do not cause the patient greater harm and contraction.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	And I myself have seen many who have applied cauterization to the ankle of the foot, and left it until the leg was completely swollen, and the foot as well, and it became pierced and corrupted throughout the entire foot.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After an abdominal solution, he died.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	And if the pain is in two parts together, apply cautery to one and the other, according to this manner.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce;	And the wise ones say about the cauterization of the spine: this is how it should be done, take a piece of iron that is as thick as a small dagger or slightly thinner, and make incisions through it, either interlaced or alternating from one side to the other, with an interval equal to the size of a thumb.
et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait;	and intertwine them over the two parts, and they should also be like new, and have a good iron made of it.
et c’est li forme:	and this is the form:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit;	and heat it until it is entirely red and emits steam, then place it on the sore hip of the patient, and turn to the healthy side.
et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors;	and apply the cautery once the heat is gone, and leave it for three days.
et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens;	and then apply an ointment of butter, and leave the wound open for a long time;
aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	after the treatment of the ointment as long as it is healed.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent;	Albuscasim says that we use this cautery little because of the fear of its reputation, and we see few who use it.
et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	and nevertheless, these are good cauterizations, which the patient can endure, and the place where it is appropriate.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi;	He uses the cautery of burning medicine if you make a tool to interweave with which you lower the edge of the door, and it is made of iron or steel on a long wall, and at the top it has two parts, and between each part there is the quantity of thickness of a finger.
et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	and they should be open above and below, and join together according to this form.
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche;	After that, place the board of the harness on the sick person lying on their side, and quickly put your hand over the board of the harness.
aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	After pouring between the two circles of hot awes (ash or charred material) heated over fire, leave it for an hour while the patient endures the heat and burn.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu;	Because it has the same effect as fire.
et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit;	and when the blisters have passed, take a clean hand with the instrument and raise the bandage of soft ash, leaving it for three days, and apply butter until the blackening from the burn is removed.
et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait;	and leave it for three days as the purification takes effect.
et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	and this is the rear support after the treatment of wounds until they are healed.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument;	And if the pain extends to the thigh or leg, use the instrument that heals according to what you have done in increasing the hip.
et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	and this is the method of hot water, which I have written about in treating rectal medicine.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Take alkali and live chalk, in equal amounts from each, and grind them together, and put them into a new pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir;	or if it has a small opening, slightly larger than the tip of a razor, so that it can be entered.
et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main;	and place this over the affected area, well-packed, and put it on an alkali and hot compress, gently pressing until there are two layers of powder above it in your hand.
et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	and leave it thus until the heat and moisture have completely dissipated, or as much as it can be packed, then take all that heat and pour it into hot water on an alkali as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres.	And thus, it will be very beneficial and useful in many medical emergencies and other cauterization of different members.
Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	For it performs the same action as fire, and if combined with other medications such as heat, poultices, honey, anacardium, and chalk with soap, all these things mixed together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	And Gallien tells us of a cure for a noble who suffered from the pain of sciatica and stiffness in the back, and he said that no other remedy was used, and that the patient was completely healed just once when this treatment was applied, and he recommended bathing as follows...
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie;	And prepare it in this manner: you press and grind the fresh and dry galen (a medicinal substance) with a little fat, and apply it to the pained area on the shoulder, thigh, or leg, and bind it.
et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	and leave it for three hours, or until the patient no longer feels the burn.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	And then make him take a bath or a drink as long as the body is slightly warm, and make him lie down, and the pain will entirely disappear and he will be healed.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	And know that no one should use fire cautery with such remedies, unless after the evacuation of the body.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout;	And Dioscorides says that when the sciatic vein is cauterized with goat's fur, it helps greatly.
et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	and the cautery must be done in this manner.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take lint and grease it with old oil, and apply it to the fossa between the big toe and the one called the hallux.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains;	After taking dry goat's fur, ignite it with fire until it becomes charcoal, and place it on the wool, leaving it until it is stained.
et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee;	and do this again, and do not cease doing so until you think by sense that it reaches the hamstring and the pain ceases.
et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	and these kinds of cauterization are called "fire cautery".
de la dolor dou dos	Of the great pain in the back
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When great pain comes to the back, whether from striking or pressure, or from excessive evacuation, or from some similar cold, expanding substance, none of these signs warrants cautery, except for that which comes from the infusion of cold material.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir;	It is necessary that after the patient is relieved of putrid pills or other similar substances, that one makes three signs on their back, neck, or wherever the pain persists, with five cauterizations or more, according to the virtue and quantity that the patient can endure.
et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»;	and the cauterizations should be made according to the cautery called "point".
et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	and if you see, make three or four cauterizations at the middle of the bone according to this form:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor;	This illness often comes to small children, and the signs of its onset are that they have a tight and painful almond-shaped eye when they open it, and sorrow.
et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	and you feel in the last, lower back spine and in its appearance that comes upon the other spines.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this and observe it healing, cauterize it with the cautery iron according to this form.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	The cautery should mark each part of the spine equally.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you see, cauterize around the spine with the cautery iron, making two or three lines, and let the points be close to one another.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	After treatment, keep the limb as healthy as possible according to what we have said, and be careful not to apply heat to numb any nerve pain.
de la dolor des jointes	joint pain
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere:	When the joint pain is caused by moisture that spreads to each part of the body, and when a sharp pain comes on, they call it "podagra" properly speaking; and when it is due to cold and cannot be cured by medicine, then cautery is the cure in this manner:
fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	Make the wound of cautery around the joint of the foot, and let the cautery be olive-shaped according to this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	And if it is necessary to prick on the face with a needle, make the cauterization all around with a claim of "no point.
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire;	And if the pains come up to the knees and other joints, and this happens often, then he should cauterize each knee with three cauteries or four from each part, making every cautery olive-shaped.
et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	and if you need to do more, do so, but do not hold your hand too tightly until the depth of the heart is burned.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pains descend to the knee and back, apply the cautery as we have said in its chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes;	And if the pains are in the hands, make points around the wound with two lines.
et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main;	and if there is no pain in the joints, make points on each joint and on the hair of the hand;
et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	and if the pains come up to the elbows or shoulders, cauterize each part and give good care to the patient and take medicines.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	For if you give good care and purge the flu, it will be healed by God's help.
de la routure dou syfac	From the rupture of the sinew.
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor;	When a rupture occurs in the thigh and the tendons descend to the knees, it is new, so it is important that when you see this, he does not move that leg for the day.
et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre;	and that he uses things which ease the stomach, so that the bowels descend from his stomach.
aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors;	after making him lie on his back between your hands, and commanding him to keep his breath until the boils are healed, arrange them at your will, and seal each rupture on the bone of the wrist, and mark it in every place with a sign resembling half a circle above the body.
puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	then heat the cautery with which there is this form:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	as long as it is white and exudes scent.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu;	Then reset the bones to their place;
et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier;	and the healers should place their hands upon it so that they do not return to the previous state.
et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains;	and open well the thighs of the patient, and place beneath him cushions and supports on the thighs, and others upon the feet which hold his hands.
puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os;	then place the cautery upon the sign across your entire hand, and hold it straight and firm until you reach the bone, and if you do not touch the bone the first time, repeat this another time until you do.
et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere;	and guard carefully that the boil does not burst when you perform the cautery.
que tu ne le brulasses;	so that you do not burn it;
et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	and that the patient does not die or suffer other ill effects.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And know that if you do not reach the bone with the cautery, your work is in vain.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure;	And it is necessary that the cautery for children be subtle according to their size, and for adults also as large according to their measure.
aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	after three days, cure the vein with butter until the burn is healed.
aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee;	After treating other wounds until they are healed, place the patient on his back for forty days while ensuring the wound is well sealed.
et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	and it is necessary that his movements be restricted for a long time, so that the boils do not appear when he moves around in bed.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors;	And after forty days, when he wishes to stand up, apply a well-made bandage and wear it for another forty days.
et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire;	and have good rest, work little, and guard against excessive drinking and eating, and from too much loud noise.
et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	and when he gives this instruction, he does so entirely sanely.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I will now describe the treatment for cutting in his chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	of the rupture of the abdomen
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur;	When ruptures occur in other organs and are recognized, and you see that they do not grow any more, it is necessary to perform cauterization with cautery according to its quantity, and burn one-third of the wound.
aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit;	after the treatment according to what we have said;
et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	and no of the ancients have said that one should cauterize with three-angled cautery according to this form:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	but first mark the place of the hernia with a sign, and make a line across the width of the rupture; then another from above, and hold your hand steady over the entire area where the hot iron will be applied.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	But the first cautery is lighter and more manageable.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	of ancient pain in any member
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	When pain arises in any member, whether from a fall or an injury, and this pain persists for a long time, and the cure of medicine is ineffective, then it should be cauterized with the cautery known as "point," and the cautery must be applied according to the length of the member and its smallness, and its weakness, and its strength, and its twist, and its location, and its pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien;	If he is healthy after the first cautery, that is good.
se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	If this does not help, start another cautery on the nearest limb, as it is usual for it to move and heal in that way; therefore, you must perform cauteries until the patient is healthy.
de meselerie	It appears that the term "de meselerie" is
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	These ailments are never helped by cautery alone, especially the illness that arises from the putrefaction of fluids and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief:	Can you cauterize it? Be careful if the disease is in the beginning and treat it according to what we have said in the previous discussion, without delay or hesitation, and if you doubt that the corruption might spread throughout the patient, then perform cauterization on the head.
I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous;	I cut off the tip of the nose, and the other towards the forehead at the end of the eyebrows.
et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel;	and then on the two horns, and behind on the scalp.
et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir;	and I allow the fire to burn until it reaches the bone, and until the skin peels away so that the vapors of the thick humors can escape.
et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	and apply the cautery to the mouse according to what is before it.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse;	And if the disorder is scattered everywhere;
et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules;	and it is evident that you need to apply these cauterizations that we have mentioned above, and cauterize the first one near the wound, and the second on the spine of the neck, and the sixth on the spine of the back, and the first on the thigh, and another delicate one, and the second on both shoulders.
et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains;	and the second on the sides, and the second on the tendons of the hand, and the first on each joint of the hands and feet, and in the pits of the hands.
et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler;	and guard the nerves that are on the lower side, stepping on them, so you do not burn them.
et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	and never perform cauterization on the bones of the fingers, or any other bones, such as those of the stomach, or the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite;	And know that the more cauterization is performed, the greater the aid, and the greater the benefit it brings.
et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	and know that the patient feels no pain from cauterization as a healthy person would, because the body is already corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	And it is necessary that the cauterization be great or small according to the members and joints, as you will find in the ways of iron.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	After treatment, apply flour of grains with honey and other remedies until it is healthy.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre;	When swelling appears in any member and is cured by medicines, oils, and bandages, but it does not heal completely, then one should perform cautery on the affected member according to its size and the severity of the condition.
et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur;	and the cautery should be performed slightly inside the heart's chamber.
puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	then attend to the wounds until they are healed.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure;	And one should never perform cautery on the hand, foot, or back, at the end of the nerve that supplies the member, and thus if the swelling is removed.
et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	and nevertheless, no one should interfere if they are not knowledgeable about the members and the passages of the moving nerves in the body.
de albaras	Of albaras (albaras could refer to a
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color;	When the disease called "albaras" is ignited, and the medical arts are powerless against it, then cauterize with a hot iron, according to the extent of the pain, until the blanching is removed, and the color returns.
puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie;	then apply a cure of meal and lentils with rose oil, plantain leaves, collicon (a herb) and alder bark, each in a portion.
et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	and mix it with everything, tie it with a cloth, and keep it elevated until it is healed.
li cure de chancre par cautere	The treatment of a ulcer (chancre) by cauterization.
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When a ulcer appears at the beginning, and you wish to stop it, cauterize it with the cautery that seems like a circle around the entire edge of the ulcer.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre;	Yet wise ones say that cautery should also be done in the middle of the cancer.
et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois;	However, this does not seem good to me, as I am afraid it might ulcerate and corrupt, and I have never seen it work before.
et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	And the more correct thing is that it should be cauterized around, in the cautery called "circle," as we have said in many cauteries.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	from the swelling that cannot die
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens;	When anyone has a disease called "adubelati," and it takes time to die, either because of the excess it produces or due to the old age of the patient when they are weak (i.e., too much), and there is little blood, or because of the time;
et tu la vues haster de meurer:	and you see it hasten to die:
adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant;	then cauterize around it with small cauteries by pricking;
aprés le laisse ensi.	afterward leave it thus.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	Because it will hasten to die.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you see it piercing through all the cauterization, make the cautery so hot that this is its shape:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	And place your hand in the midst of this ill-named 'adubelati' disease until the cauterizer has perceived the heart, and it is arranged as the cauterizer wishes, so that the patient feels freed in such a way that the course of the decay is halted.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	After the cure, until it is perfectly healed.
li cure dou feu par fer	Heal the fire with iron.
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	Another type of disease is called 'corrodens', which is nothing other than a corruption of the limbs, as it attacks the members just as fire does the dry wood.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est;	If you see this disease in a limb that can be treated with fire cautery, then heat the cautery instruments slightly and greatly, according to what is suitable for the limb or the illness.
aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	After cauterizing all parts until you eliminate all corruption, and nothing remains of it, everything that is corrupted must be removed.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	Then leave it for three days, and apply oil to the cauterized limb suffering from broying until all the burns from the fire are removed, and all the corruption.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	After the treatment of wounds that cause pain.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin;	And if after three days you see no sign of healing, that is good.
et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	and if that is not the case, then repeat the cautery on what remains of the limb that has been corrupted.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu;	And this dislocation is sometimes cured with hot medicines instead of fire cautery;
mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division:	But nevertheless, fire cautery is of greater help, and I have already spoken about the treatment with hot medicines in the previous section.
pren la quant tu en as mestier.	take as much as you need.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	from the vessels that come as pieces
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	Many times it happens that a piece due to deficiency develops a disease called "close" according to our intention, and it is a great fault that damages the foot.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And the treatment for this illness is according to two methods.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	This refers to fire cautery and hot water cautery.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges;	For fire cautery, if you are skilled in it, it is like sewing with a needle, also as thin as a feather, and made of good iron to fit the size so that it can pierce the skin from all sides and have subtle edges.
aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou;	After applying all heat to the nail, and turning your hand around the nail until it reaches the bottom of the nail;
et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture;	and leave it like this for three days until it begins to fester;
puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	then make a poultice of sage leaves ground with string, and leave the poultice on all night; the nail will come off and be pulled out from its roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat the shoulder with a healing ointment, making it clean and sound.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude;	And if they are burned by fire and many times occur in hands and feet, then it is necessary to apply a hot water cautery to them.
et est en teil maniere:	and it is in this way:
pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues;	take a cane of iron or wood, or a feather from a pigeon, and place the nail and the glue, that is to say, the wart-removing paste.
et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine;	and place the cane around it so that it envelops everything, then apply a little hot ash, and hold your hand firmly, and press your hand while twisting until the edge of the cane reaches the root of the nail, and can find the hot water channel all the way to the root.
et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre;	and make the patient suffer a little the bite of hot water for an hour;
puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	then leave it thus, and it will pull out at the roots entirely.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	First, make one after another, until you straighten all those that are in the body, then treat the wounds that cause harm.
li cure dou trembler	It cures the shivering.
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee;	When anyone shivers from cold or trembles with quartan fever or any other illness, it is necessary that you make four cauterizations or five along the spine, one cauterization between each spine;
et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire;	and make one cauterization on the foot, and another on the stomach with an olive cautery;
si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	if he lets it shake, and hastens the health of the cold disease.
des pustules puans	from the pus-filled blisters
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	Never is the body's health apparent through external baths or pus-filled blisters, which come from deeply corrupt materials.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule:	it is necessary at first to know when they appear that we make cautery on each head of the pustule:
un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	a subtle cautery with hot charcoal, so that the point is taken to the fire, or with a long root of aristologus, or with lenticular cautery.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez;	And under no circumstances should cautery be performed at the beginning when they appear, according to this manner, and they cannot grow worse in front, but it breaks the excess from which they come, and heals;
mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	but it must be done after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	when the artery is cut off
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses;	Many times there occur great complications from the blood of an artery that is cut during a wound, or at the complete healing, or during cauterization of a member, and similar things.
et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	and it is a very serious matter to stink.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus;	And nevertheless, if it happens to anyone, be quick to place your index finger on the wound of the vein, and hold it very tightly until the pain is completely relieved from beneath your finger, and no more blood flows.
puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge;	then apply to the fire various olive oil cauterizing tools, both small and large, until they are entirely red.
puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	then take, according to the size of the wound and the location where the artery flows, either a large or small cauterizing tool, and place it on the vein where you hold your finger, keeping the cauterizing tool there until the blood stops flowing.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement I autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	And if a sudden leap occurs while you are lying with your arm over the vein, and the cauterization is complete, then quickly take another cautery from the fire.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez;	and do not stop doing this one after another until the blood stops flowing.
et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide;	and be careful not to burn the nerve that is nearby, and ensure no further harm comes to the patient.
et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit:	and know that when there is no bleeding from the artery, one cannot properly feel it, especially when the artery is large, unless by one of the three ways we have mentioned.
ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc;	or by cauterization, or by extraction when it is not treated, or by tightly wrapping it with thread, or by medications applied that have the power to stop blood flow.
et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	and it becomes stiff and constricted.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	Whoever administers relief to a tight closure with cloths or places burning objects or similar things on it, will not be successful unless he does it carefully.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne;	And if this happens to anyone and they have no suitable medication, they should place their two fingers on the wound of the vein as we have said, and tightly compress it until blood stops flowing from the wound and the vein.
et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez;	and do not move it, but moisten it with cold water often as it becomes very cold until the flesh is frozen and swollen and numb.
et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	and make inquiries about those who need cautery and medicine.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	We begin the second book of surgical treatments.
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres;	We have told you in the first chapter all about the diseases for which it is necessary to use fire cautery or burning medicine, and we have explained the reasons, instruments, and forms of cautery.
et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	and I have placed this chapter on the most common problems, and I will follow the same way in this chapter so that you may find what you seek more easily.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	And so, before we begin, it is necessary for you to know that this chapter involves greater risk and fear than the first one on cautery, and therefore requires more careful attention.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses;	For in the work of this chapter, there is often the evacuation of blood when opening a vein, and incising an abscess, and in the treatment of wounds, and in the extraction of arrows, and in cutting into stones, and similar things;
ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	where there is doubt and fear, and many die.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	And I warn you not to undertake foolishness.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	For many ways of people come for cure.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice;	if they come from those who have become so accustomed to their illness that they die gently due to the severity of their condition and the magnitude of their suffering.
et de ces doit on avoir paor.	and from these one must fear.
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit:	And of these there are those who give you their trust, and say:
«atendez, je sui garis»;	Wait, I am tired.
et li maladie est despitouse.	and the illness is spiteful.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los;	You should not agree to those who come to you with this manner, but put more great caution in your honor than in your greed, and do not act rashly but wisely regarding what is certain to you, and what you can safely take and let go of.
et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie;	and use divination and indication in the treatment of your patients so that health is restored.
et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	and this will help you gain good reputation, glory, and lasting fame.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	Most precious child, Our Lords give you good understanding and rectitude, and if you desire the holy inspiration from His hand, amen.
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	Or I have ordered this chapter for you, reflecting on chapters of surgery, according to the one that is before or at the end of the chapter on cautery, which I have devised from head to foot, so that you may find it easier to understand what you will need.
dou chief plein d’aigue	Dou chief plein d'aigue" translates to "a head full of blood
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant;	Know that this illness often comes to children at birth, and when the head is squeezed too tightly.
et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	and never comes from a known cause, as we do not know.
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors;	And I have never seen this disease except in children, and to all those that I have seen, death has come quickly.
et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	and for this reason, it seems to me that I should abandon the work in part, regarding certain treatments.
Et je vis I enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir;	And I saw children with their joints filled with water, and the head swelled each day until it could no longer be borne.
et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os;	and the moisture was so great that it became death, and this moisture is gathered beneath the skin over the bone in the region of the heart and the bone.
et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large;	and if the work is such that moisture is between the heart and the bone, and the abscess is small, you must make a wide cut with your knife through the skull.
et soit ausi longe com II nous, tant que li mostor corre;	and it should be as long as the moisture runs.
et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	and see here the form of the spatula:
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai II fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	If the moisture is more severe, and the abscess larger, make two cuts in the shape of a cross, according to this form:
Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut:	And if the moisture is beneath the bone, and you see the openings of the skull's crevices clearly, and there is a sharp, strong pain when you press your hand inside, and it does not return:
si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief III fendures selonc ceste maniere:	If you wish to cut into the head, make three incisions according to this manner:
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	And after the incision, remove all the moisture completely.
Aprés estraint les fendures de drapelz et de poudres, et i met vin et oile, et laisse ensi jusc’a cinquieme jor;	After making the incisions, close them with bandages and powders, and then apply wine and oil, leaving it for up to five days.
puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.	then open it, treat the wound with bandages and compresses, and further dislocate the head equally, allowing the patient to eat dry meat from a bag of moisture until the limb is comfortable and healed.
Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue;	And another method of incision is to observe the size of the abscess and the collection of pus.
car aucune fois est elle devant;	for never is she before;
aucune fois derrier;	not once behind;
aucune fois en destre;	never once on the right;
et aucune fois en senestre.	and never once on the left.
Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir;	Then cut open the abscess, and drain the pus, and make an opening according to your ability.
et warde que tu ne coper l’artere;	and be sure not to cover the artery;
et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.	and draw out the blood flow with a smooth motion, so that the patient does not die from the sudden influx of blood and the evacuation of moisture.
de reume	Of the root
Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les II arteres.	When someone has a condition called "cataract" in one or both eyes, and the disease is old, and medical treatment does not help, then the final remedy is cauterization by sealing the two arteries.
Il covient donques, cant tu les vues coper, que li malaides faice rere son chief;	It is therefore necessary, when you see them cover their eyes, that the patient turns his head back.
aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel;	after rubbing the affected area with a rough cloth until the arteries open, then carefully extract the patient's collar with all the cloth.
puis regarde ou li voine bait, et li leus de l’une et de l’autre sont aprés les oreilles, et poc sont reponues;	then look at where the vein is located, and the joints on both sides are behind the ears, and they are properly repositioned.
puis signe les leus d’enche, puis cope l’une et l’autre d’un spatumile agut de II pars, tant que li taille veigne jusc’a l’os, et ceu soit par lou large dou chief.	then mark the joints with signs, then cut one and both with a sharp spatula, reaching as far as the bone, and this should be done from the wide end upwards.
Et se tu vues, boute le spatumile desoz l’artere et la cope au desus, en taillant ausi com II dois au traver.	And if you see, remove the spatule beneath the artery and cut through the covering above, cutting as it should go through.
Et quant li voinne est copee, si saut li sans en haut continuelment fuers.	And when the vein is cut, it bleeds continuously from above.
Et se li artere n’apert au sentir, si covient que tu mesures la quantiteit de l’espaice de III dois, puis seigne d’enche et fent jusc’a l’os;	and if the artery does not open upon stimulation, it is necessary that you measure the quantity of space with three fingers, then mark it with a sign and cut through to the bone.
et ceu qu’il covient dou sanc mettre fuers si est VI c/, et par aventure un poc plus ou moins, selonc ce que li malaides puet soffrir, et la repletion de l’artere;	and that one should put the cautery over the blood if it is six parts deep, and perhaps a little more or less, according to what the patient can endure, and the filling of the artery.
puis regarde la plaie:	then examine the wound:
s’il remaint sus l’os point dou syphac, si le cope que apostemes chaus n’i veigne, puis estrain la plaie et lie, et la cure d’oignement tant qu’ele soit sanee.	if it remains on the bone with a hard lump, and no abscess forms, then strain the wound and bind it, and apply treatment until it is clean.
de emigrainne	from migraine headache
Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	When an old migraine headache occurs, accompanied by catarrh, due to moisture in the eyes and sockets, and ancient fatigue and similar symptoms, it is treated with various medical cures, but often without success. Therefore, we drain the arteries of the eyes and apply cautery, as we have described.
Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit;	And the method of extracting them is that the patient pulls out the hairs from his temples, and finds the artery that opens in the temple, as it opens well with its beating, and is hardly closed outside that no other men who are too weak can do.
et s’elle est reponue, si estraigne son col li malaides d’aucuns drapelz, puis frote le leu d’aucun aspre drap, et arose le leu d’aigue chaude tant que li artere apere manifestement;	and if it is reduced, the patient should pull on the collar with some cloth, then rub the joint with a rough cloth and immerse it in hot water until the artery becomes clearly visible.
puis pren le spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	then take the spatula with its shape:
puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie;	then scrape the skin lightly until you feel the artery, then hold it with pliers and remove all the threads that adhere to each part.
et se li artere est subtilz, si la torne a la pointe de l’uncine, puis la cope de celle partie selonc la quantiteit des II chiés.	and if the artery is thin, return it to the tip of the hook and cut off that part according to the number of joints.
Car s’elle n’est copee, si ne saut mie li sans dou tout en tout.	For if it is not cut, it does not heal at all without pain.
Et trai dou sanc des VI c/, jusc’a III;	And extract the blood from six vessels, up to three times.
et se li artere est grans, si covient que tu la lies en II leus d’un fil double fort de soie, que porriture n’i veigne devant le soudement de la plaie, et veigne decorremens de sanc;	and if the artery is large, it is necessary that you bind it in two places with a strong double thread of silk, to prevent any leakage before the wound heals, and to avoid further bleeding.
puis cope la superfluiteit qui est entre les II liiens en celle houre meisme, et puis, se tu vues, si lou cauterize dou cautere cutellaire jusc’a l’os tant que li chiés soient copez;	then cut off the excess between the two threads at that very moment, and then, if you see fit, cauterize with a cutting cautery instrument up to the bone, as long as the chips are removed.
et c’est li muedre oevre, se li malaides n’a fievre et il est de chaude complexion.	and this is the mother work, if the patient has fever and is of hot complexion.
Car li cauteres est aide por finir les moistors:	For cautery is helpful in ending moisture:
por ceu est il de plus grant aide as moistors.	because it is of greater help with moisture.
Ou il covient por l’estraction des arteres que om emplisse lou leu de viel coton et mette on sus tentes bien faites;	Or, for the extraction of arteries, it is appropriate to fill the wound with fine cotton and cover it with well-made bandages.
et quant on les desliera, si soit curez de medicines seches que font naistre char, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez;	and when they are unbound, take care with dry medicines that produce heat and bandages, until it is healed.
et se sans cort de l’artere tant dis com tu i oevres, si te haste dou coper par cautere, ou tu emple lou leu de vitriole et l’estrain a ta main que li sans soit estainchiez;	and without any delay of the artery as you do it, if you hurry to cover with cautery, or you use the fire of vitriol and press it in your hand so that the wound is cleansed;
et se tu n’as ceu present, si met sor le leu ton doit tant que li sans soit congelez, et arose le leu d’aigue froide tant que li sans cesse, et soit estraint si com il covient;	and if you do not have this at hand, place cold water on the wound until it is frozen, and then apply hot water until the wound is healed, and press it as needed.
et ceu qui est muedre et plus legier en l’estraction de l’artere est que tu cauterizes la voinne de cest cautere trenchant de II pars, mais li trenchant soient bien espés por warder plus longement lor chalor.	and the more mobile and lighter in the extraction of the artery is that you cauterize the vein with this sharp cautery from both sides, but the cuts should be well spaced to retain their heat for longer.
Car quant li estrumens est trop tenves, si tient moins sa chalor.	For when the instruments are too tight, they do not hold their heat.
Et doit avoir entre les II coutelz I doit de gros d’espaice, et puis quant tu as signiet d’enche les II leus, et tu mes lou fer ardant sus tant qu’il viegne jusc’a l’os, et cope la voinne en II leus;	And it should have between the two knives a space of good size, and then when you have marked with a sign both sides, and put the hot iron onto until it reaches the bone, cut the vein in two places.
et soient esloigniet entre les II chiés car il n’est mie soudez de cest cautere dou tout en tout;	and be separated between the two sides, for this cautery is not firmly attached in every way.
et c’est li forme dou cautere:	and this is the form of cautery:
des larmes	tears
Quant les larmes des eulz sont dessendans des voinnes que sont sus lou test dou chief de fuer, et il ne profite mie cure de medicine c’on i faice, et tu vois la faice dou malaide enrougir, et sent ou front ambulation si com de fremis;	When the tears from the eyes flow into the veins that are on top of the head, and no benefit is gained from the medicines applied there, and you see the face of the patient turning red, and smell a foul odor emanating from his forehead as if from a wound.
