et l’aministre en ces plaies por enjanrer char per tout.	and administer these remedies to promote healing throughout.
de l’estoupement des oreilles	From ear trauma
Tout ceu que chiet ens oreilles est une des IIII choses:	Everything that matters to the ears is one of the four things:
ou grains, ou beste, ou piere de mine ou semblans chose si com fer;	or seeds, or animals, or minerals from the earth or similar things as it were done;
ou semence, si com jaisses, feves, pois;	or seeds, such as beans, peas;
ou chose defluans si com aigue et aisilz et semblans choses.	or fluid things, as water and air, and similar things.
Quant il chiet en l’oreille piere ou autre maniere de chose que ne s’ajoste mie a l’oreille, ne ne croist en l’oreille, si met l’oreille au solel.	If anything, such as a stone or any other object that does not adjust to the ear or grow in the ear, is inserted into the ear, it should be removed and the ear exposed to sunlight.
Se tu vois la piere, si distille aucun poc d’oile violet ou oile de sisament, puis i amenistre extraction;	If you see a stone, and it distills any little drop of purple oil or oil of cloves, then it is time for extraction.
et lou fai esternuer de condisi, et li estoupe les narines quant li esternuemens vient, et met entor l’oreille pieces de drapelz ou laine;	and the cold causes sneezing, and it numbs the nostrils when sneezing occurs, and puts pieces of cloth or wool inside the ear.
et estent l’oreille au desus.	and stretches the ear upwards.
Mout de fois vient fuer par ceste cure;	Many times, this treatment causes fever.
et s’elle ne vient fuer, se li amenistre extraction as pinceures subtilz, de coi ci est li forme:	and if it does not come out, apply extraction with fine pincers, from which comes this form:
S’elle saut fuer as pinceures, c’est boin;	if it jumps out through the pincers, that is good;
se ceu non, si amenistre extraction a l’oncine subtil de petite doubleure;	if it does not, apply extraction with a fine, small-toothed instrument;
et s’elle ne saut par ceu, si fai une caine d’arain et boute lou chief de la cainne ou pertuis de l’oreille fort, et estoupe ceu qui est entor la cainne de cire mole si que li vens n’i puisse entrer avec la cainne;	and if it still does not come out, make a hook with iron and twist the hook deeply into the ear canal or ear hole, and stuff soft wax around the hook so that the wind cannot enter through the hook;
puis le trai fuer forment, car mout de fois vient fuer si com nos avons dit;	then take him to a skilled surgeon, for many times it comes about as we have said;
et s’elle ne vient fuer en teil maniere, si prent glut de coi en prent les oisiaus, et met en som aucun estrument qui soit a point por ceu faire, et met un poc de coton entor;	and if it does not come about in this way, then grasp it firmly with your hands and use any sharp instrument to do so, and place a bit of cotton around.
puis presse le glut sus la piere ou quel chose que ce soit, et trai fuer.	then press the lump against the stone or something else, and treat it.
Et s’elle ne saut fuer de toutes ces choses que nos avons dit, si te haste de fendre l’oreille ainsois que aposteme chalz i veigne, et spasme;	And if none of the things we have said work, then quickly split the ear in such a way that the abscess hardens and stops moving.
et li maniere de la fendure si est que tu faices premier sainier lou malaide de la cephalique, et estrai dou sanc selonc la mesure de sa vertu, puis fai seoir lou malaide entre tes mains et li torne l’oreille au desus, et fent une petite fendure en la racine de l’oreille a la graisse ou leu dependant;	and the method of the cut is that you first dress the patient with the disease in the head, extract the blood according to its quality, then place the patient between your hands and return the ear to its place, and make a small cut at the base of the ear where the fat or tissue is attached.
et soit li fendure ausi com une lune, tant que tu viegnes a la piere, puis l’oste selonc ton pooir, et la suce hastanment a ta bouche;	and make the cut as thin as a moon, until you reach the bone, then remove it according to your ability, and suck it gently with your mouth.
et la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and treat it while it is healthy.
Et se c’est grains qui est ens et il enfle, si aministre extraction;	And if there are grains that are embedded and they swell, then administer extraction.
et si’il ne puet issir, si amenistre I spatumile tenve subtil selonc ceste forme:	and if it cannot be extracted, then administer the delicate scraping according to this form:
et amenistre incision de celui grain.	and make an incision of that grain.
Mais ne faire mie ceu quant tu penses que li grains est moistes por la moistor de l’oreille, tant que tu en aies fait maintes pieces;	But do not attempt this if you think the grains are moist from earwax, as long as you have made many attempts.
puis l’estrai as pinceures subtilz et au succier, si com nos avons dit, si que li estractions soit aligie.	then extract them with delicate tweezers and suction, as we have said, so that the extraction is light.
En l’aigue donques que chiet en l’oreille covient que li malaides use d’esternuement de condisi premiers, et ample l’oreille de viel coton.	In the case that something has entered the ear, have the patient use a gentle sneeze, and open the ear with old cotton.
Et soit gisans sus celle oreille meisme ou li aigue est.	And lie down on that same ear, or the water is inside.
s’elle saut fuer per ceu, c’est boin.	If she jumps through the fire, it is good.
se ceu non, si prent maintes pieres selonc li longesce de ton doit tenves et legieres, et les eschaufe un poc au feu;	if indeed you take many needles according to the length of your thumb, and hold them slightly warm over fire.
et em mette li malaides une ou pertus de son oreille, et saille sus i. de ses piez d’autre part, et fiere d’une autre piere sus la piere qui est en l’oreille;	and then place the patient in a pit or hole on his side, and try from another direction, and strike with another stone on the stone that is inside the ear.
et ne cesse de faire ceu de piere em piere tant que li aigue isse toute fuer, et ensi saut elle toute fuer;	and continue to strike one stone with another until the blood completely flows out, and thus it will completely come out.
et se tu vues, si prent I jonc, et boute l’un des chiés en l’oreille, et l’autre chief emprent de feu tant que li plus dou jonc soit ars;	and if you see, take a thin strip, and insert one of the openings into the ear, and burn the other end over fire until the thinner strip is completely charred.
puis refai autreteil d’autres jons tant que li aigue isse toute, si com nos avons dit en la piere.	Then make other preparations from different joints until the pain completely disappears, as we said before.
En l’estraction de la beste, s’elle est de petit cors, si com puce et semblans chose, cure la si com nos avons dit en la division;	When extracting a small creature, such as a tiny pest or similar thing, treat it as we described in the previous section.
mais s’elle est de grant cors c’on la puisse sentir, si amenistre extraction de pinceures;	but if it is large and can be felt, extract it with tweezers.
et c’est li chose plus legiere a oster qui soit en l’oreille.	and it is the easiest thing to remove, which is in the ear.
En l’estraction des vers enjanrez as oreilles, quant tu lou cures si com nos avons dit en la division et ou traitier des distillations, et li cure ne profite mie, si covient que tu regardes l’oreille au soleil:	During the extraction of worms from the ears, when you treat it as we have said in the section on dealing with distillations, and the cure does not benefit, then you must examine the ear in the sunlight.
s’il i apert nulz vers, si les trai as pinceures subtilz, et s’il n’aperent, si prent la cainne de coi ci est li forme:	If no worms open, using delicate pincers, and if they do not open, take the cane from which their shape is thus revealed.
Et soit estroite desoz et large desus.	And it should be tight from below and wide from above.
Et boute lou plus subtil chief en l’oreille selonc la quantiteit de la soffrance dou malaide, puis succe forment a tot la caine;	And insert the most delicate instrument into the ear according to the amount of suffering of the patient, then suction along the entire cane.
fai ceu sovent tant que tuit li ver issent.	Do this often until all the wounds are healed.
Et s’il n’obeissent a issir, si estoupe entor la cainne de coton si com j’ai dit en la piere;	And if they do not obey in coming out, cut around the wound with a cotton thread as I have said before.
et s’il ne saillent fuer si com nos avons dit, si aministre distillations que li ancien ont esprovees en l’ocision des vers, et tu les troveras ou traitier des distillations;	and if they do not come out as we have said, administer distillations that the ancients have tested in treating worm infections, and you will find them discussed under distillations.
et si distille tes oiles et tes medicines en l’oreille a tout cest estrument, de coi ci est li forme si com tu vois:	and if you distill your oils and medicines into the ear using all these instruments, it will take the form as you see:
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain estrois desoz a I petis pertuis, et desus overs por distiller;	And whether it is of silver or gold, make thin plates from small openings to distill above.
et por presser dedens la distillation a I estrument d’arain bien fait por ceu, et se tu vues pren I raseur et envoloupe entor la pointe avenanment coton;	and to press the distillation down with a well-made silver instrument for this purpose, and if you see that it sticks, take a razor and wrap cotton around the tip carefully.
puis i giete ton oile ou ton jus, et ceu que tu vues de tes medicines en la cainne, et li caine soit en l’oreille;	then pour your oil or juice, and whatever you see of your medications in the cauldron, and place the cauldron in the ear.
puis boute dedens lou raseur a tout lou coton, et presse ta main tempreement tant que li oile soit distilleit ou chevement de l’oreille;	then put the razor completely into the cotton and press your tempered hand until the oil is distilled or slightly from the ear.
et lou sente li malaides dedens, et soit li distillations I poc eschaufee au feu ainsois c’on la distille en l’oreille;	and he feels the patient within, and let there be distillations from fire so that they are heated by the flame just as one distills in the ear;
et garde qu’elle ne soit trop froide, car li medicine ne seroit mie si bone.	and ensure it is not too cold, for the medicine would not be as good.
de l’estoupement des oreilles	From ear trauma
Aucun enfant naissent qui n’ont nul pertus ens oreilles;	No child is born with any holes in their ears.
et ceste meisme chose avient as homes par estoupement de plaie, ou de char nee dedens l’oreille, et cist estoupemens vient aucune fois em parfont en l’oreille, si c’on ne lou puet veoir;	and the same thing happens to adults due to a wound or a foreign object in the ear, and this blockage never completely blocks the ear unless one can see it.
et aucune fois avient I poc defuer lou pertus, et lou voit om bien.	and never does there come a time when the wound is too deep, and the sight is good.
Celle donques que vient em parfont, si c’on ne la puet veoir, est de grief sanation em plusors dispositions, et en cele c’on voit covient que tu mettes l’oreille dou malaide au soleil;	When, therefore, it comes to perfection, if one cannot see it, it is a great misfortune for the patient, and requires various remedies. And in this case, you must put the ear of the patient towards the sun.
et regarde dedens:	and look inside:
se tu vois l’opilation apparent, si la oevre a tot cest spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	if you see the swelling is evident, and the work has all these contours, then this is the shape:
Et soit agus et trenchans devant et derrier tout plain, si qu’il ne blece l’oreille;	And make incisions and cuts all around, both front and back, so that the ear is not damaged.
se li opilation est de char nee ou cors de l’oreille, si la tien as pinceures subtilz, et la cope legierement, tant que celle chars soit toute ostee.	if the operation is from within or at the base of the ear, and you have fine tweezers, hold it gently and pull it slightly until the whole pin is extracted.
Et se li opilations est em parfont en l’oreille, si pren I raseur subtil legier et l’eschaufe un petit au feu, puis li met ou cors de l’oreille.	If the infection is completely within the ear, take a fine, sharp razor, heat it slightly over fire, and insert it into the ear.
Se tu sens l’opilation dont li malaides sent grieteit a l’oïr, perce legierement, et garde que tu ne grever les ners de l’oreille;	If you feel the operation causing great pain in the ear, make a slight incision and be careful not to hurt the nerves of the ear.
puis met en l’oreille une tente selonc la largesce dou pertus, et la moille en l’oignement egyptien.	then place in the ear a piece of cloth according to the width of the opening, and dampen it with Egyptian ointment.
Fai ceu aucun jor tant que li plaie soit soudee, ou tu pren une tente et la moille en aigue rose, et poudre sus vitriole broiet;	Make no movement until the wound is healed, or take a cloth and soak it in rosewater, and sprinkle it with powder made from crushed vitriol.
et se tu vois enflee l’oreille, si couvient que tu traies la tente et remue une autre tente moillie en cerote qui soit fait d’oile roset et de cire, tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	and if you see the ear swollen, it is necessary that you dry the cloth and use another moistened cloth made of rose oil and wax, until the swelling is gone.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat it as long as it is clean.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si plonge une esponge et drapelz en aigue froide, et le met sus l’oreille, et use d’autres cures qui oste lou decorrement de sanc qui sont ou traitier des destillations.	And if bleeding occurs, dip a sponge and cloth in cold water, place it on the ear, and use other treatments to stop the bleeding, which include using distillation remedies.
de la char des papieres	concerning the use of papers
Cist althelul que vienent em papieres des eulz quant ils sont moiste et sont sec, si covient que tu les estendes de tenailles et de pinceures, et le cope d’un spatumile de ses racines;	Consider all those that come in papers when they are moist and dry, it is necessary that you extend them with tweezers and pincers, and cut off a piece of its root with a spatula.
puis met sor le leu vitriole broiet.	Then place a hot glass (or 'vitriole' in Old French) on it.
Et se sans en decort, si le cauterize dou cautere lenticulaire subtil, et li cauterizeir aprés l’incision vaut mues;	And if, after removing the skin, you cauterize with a delicate lenticular heat, and the cauterizer moves after incision;
et maintes fois repairent, cant aucune chose demoure de lor racines;	and often they heal, but nothing stays rooted in its place;
et quant elles sont cauterizees par feu, si sont arses celles racines et ne revienent mie.	and when they are cauterized with fire, their roots are burned and do not return.
de la gresle	(without context it's difficult to provide an accurate translation, but based
Maintes fois vienent em papieres des eulz unes choses que semblent gresle en sa forme et en sa duresce, et por ceu est ceste maladie apelee «grandine», et est une assemblee de moistor grosse en la papiere desus et desoz;	Many times come to paper some things that seem gravely in their form and hardness, and for this reason this disease is called "hail," and it is a gathering of great moisture on the paper above and below.
li ovraiges est telz:	The work is as follows:
pren warde se li grandine se muet d’une part et d’autre, et c’est legiere chose a savoir;	take care that the hail is silent on both sides, and this is a light thing to know;
fent la donques dou large, puis l’escorche de chescune partie legierement, puis la prent as pinceures, et la cope.	then make the cut deep, then peel gently from each part, then take them with pincers and cut.
se tu ne la pues coper sens percier un poc la papiere, si ne grieve rien au malaide;	if you cannot cover it without piercing the paper slightly, then it will not harm the patient.
et se li fendure est grans, si l’assemble a une costure, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee;	and if the fracture is large, and the assembly has a seam, treat it until it is healed.
et s’elle est petite, si n’i faire point de force, car li oignemens la restoure tantost et enjanre char.	and if it is small, do not apply too much strength, because the bruises will quickly restore themselves and cause pain.
Et se li grandine est dessendans au dedens de l’oreille vers la partie desus, si enverse la papiere, et estent la grandine a unes pinceures, et la cope et presse d’une part et d’autre;	And if the pain radiates downwards inside the ear towards the top, turn the paper in that direction, and use pliers to hold the ice, cutting and pressing on both sides.
et se li papiere est esloignie par l’incision, ce ne grieve rien;	and if the paper is separated by the incision, it causes no harm.
et quant li grandine est copee, si leive l’oil d’aigue salee, et cure le leu de ceu qui enjanre char tant que li malaides soit sanez.	and when the pain is severe, leave the oil of salt water, and heal the wound of the one who suffers until the patient is well.
de la graisse des eulz	from the fat of the eyes
Exinach est une graisse qui est enjanree en toiles des papieres desus, et ce avient plus as enfans c’a nules gens, et grieve mout a lor eulz, et li vienent li catharre as matinees, et ne pueent regardeir la lumiere dou soleil por ceu que les larmes se hastent a lor eulz;	Xerophthalmia is a fat that is deposited on the surfaces of papers, and this happens more often in children than in adults, causing them great suffering, leading to cataracts in the morning, and they cannot bear the light of the sun because tears rush to their eyes.
et por ceu se couchent il sor lor faices adés, et dorment sus, et sont lor papieres desoz lor sorcilz moistes que li enfleure et li apparance ont covert de l’exinach qui apert en l’oil.	and for this reason, they lay their face down and sleep on it, and their eyes become moist under their eyelids, which inflames and changes the appearance of the skin due to the oil.
Et quant tu presses lou leu a tes dois et sent l’exirnach entr’ous.	And when you press the joint with your fingers and feel the exit between them.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain;	And the method of this work is that the patient places his head in a healthy position;
et puis pren I drapeil de lin, et appareille une tente em maniere d’un cercle selonc la quantiteit que conteigne exirnach de chescune partie, puis le met sus li;	and then take the linen cloth, and make a tent in a circular manner according to the quantity of each part's extirpation, and place it over them.
et presse a tes dois d’une part et d’autre, si que li exirnach soit assemblez emmi le cercle;	and press with your hands on both sides so that the bone is brought together within the circle.
puis fent em mileu de la moistor au spatumile trenchant une fendure dou large, et ne soit mie plus grans que li plaie c’on fait a la sainie de voinne;	then make a groove in the middle of the moisture with a sharp scalpel, not wider than the wound made on a vein.
et fent le cuir em parfont tant que tu veignes a l’exirnach;	and cut the skin completely until you reach the bone.
et em plusors dispositions vient exirnach de la fendure, selonc la forme d’une piece de graisse blainche.	and from the groove, with various arrangements, pull out in the shape of a white fat piece.
Estrai la donques a tout une piece de drap charpit entre tes dois au defuer, et torne ta main a destre et a senestre tant qu’il soit espars;	Take a whole piece of cloth dipped in hot water between your fingers and turn your hand to the right and left as long as it is warm.
et garde que tu n’ajoster en la fendure, que tu ne viegnes a tout le spatumile jusc’a l’oil, que tu ne le bleces.	and ensure that you do not pry open the gap, that you reach all the way to the bottom without pressing too hard, and do not cause it to bleed.
Et se li exirnach n’apert en l’encomencement de la fendure, si acroi un poc la fendure legierement tant qu’il apere;	And if the gap does not open at the beginning, gently widen it a little until it opens.
puis l’estrai si com nos avons dit, puis moille drapelz en aisil et en aigue, et met sus le leu, et estrain de bendelz.	then pull it out as we have said, then moisten cloth with oil and water, place it on the joint, and stretch it gently.
Et si a de tels homes qui broient seil et mettent sus por corrompre cele moistor qui est demoree.	And if there are such people who grind and apply something to corrupt the moisture that is stuck.
Puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat it as long as it remains healthy.
Et s’il vient au leu aposteme chaut, si lou cure d’emplaustres assouajant tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if it comes to the hot abscess, treat it with external plasters soothing as long as it remains healthy.
des poilz des papieres	hairs of paper
Quant em papieres naissent poilz ajostez autre que li naturez, et sont enveillit, si nuisent as eulz, et font venir manieres de maladies si com larmes acostumees et mollifications des papieres et albugine, tant que c’est cause de la destruction des eulz;	When papers (hairs) grow in an abnormal way and become tangled, they are just as harmful, causing conditions like normal tears and soft or flaky skin, due to the damage done to the hair itself.
et est li cure selonc IIII manieres:	and the treatment is according to four methods:
ou par cautere ensamble feu, ou par medicine ague selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre de cautere, et est fais ou par incision et costure ou par caines, selonc ceu que je dirai.	or by cauterization with fire, or by using remedies according to the condition presented, or chapter on cauterization, and it is performed by incision and stitching, or by bindings, as I will explain.
Il covient que tu mettes lou chief dou malaide en ton sain, puis torne la papiere de l’oil a ta main senestre;	It is necessary that you place the patient's head in your hands, then turn the paper from the oil to your left hand.
s’elle est convertie, c’est boin;	if it turns out well, that is good.
se ceu non, si i boute une aguille a tout I fil desus;	if no, then push an needle through all the thread above it.
et soit ce delez la marge de la papiere ou li poil naissent delez ces poilz, et trai I fil au desus a tout la papiere, et la torne au raseur;	and it should be smooth along the edge of the paper where the hairs grow, and pull the thread through all the paper, and turn it to the razor.
puis fent en la partie desoz la papiere, desoz les poilz ajostez, a tout le spatumile copant, des le grant larmier jusc’au petit;	Then, peeling off the skin from the affected area, separate the hairs, gently pulling them from the base, all the way to the tip, from the great tear to the small.
puis estrai I fil, et met desoz la papiere une petite tente de couton et de drapeil, puis seigne sus la papiere une figure d’enche, si com la fuelle de mirte, et toutevoie il covient que li figure soit selonc la quantiteit que tu vues eslever la papiere qui est devisez a toz.	Then, extract the thread and place a small piece of cotton and linen paper underneath it, then trace on the paper an enche shape (a type of hook), similar to a mirte leaf, and ensure that the shape is according to the quantity you see the paper rise to.
Et si a teil qui a mestier c’on cope grant quantiteit de la papiere selonc ceu que li papiere est mollifie;	And if at that part where the skill is, much paper is needed according to how soft the paper is.
puis fent a tout le spatumile sus les II lignes que tu as signiet, et comence des lou grant larmier jusc’a petit;	then make incisions across the entire split at the marked places on both lines, beginning with a large tear from above to below.
et soit li une des fendures pres des poilz naturez en la groissece d’un raiz, puis boute l’oncine en l’un des II angles dou keur, puis l’escorche toute;	and it should be one of the splits near the natural hairs, making it as thick as a root, then turn the hook in one of the two angles towards the heart, and then peel it entirely.
puis assemble les II levres a une costure d’une aguille a tout I fil de laine subtil, et essue le sanc, et fai aerdre la superfluiteit des filz sus les II sorcilz a tout aucunes choses gluans, se tu vues faire ce;	then join the two lips with a stitch using a thin needle and thread, wipe away the blood, and remove any excess thread from between the two edges without anything sticky, if you are able to do this.
et se ce non, si n’en aies cure, puis laisse la costure et les filz jusc’a III jors ou IIII;	and if this does not help, then after leaving the stitching and threads for three or four days, or even longer.
puis cure la plaie sens costure de choses sechans et constrignans, car li papiere se relive au soudement de la plaie et l’assemblement de li, mais li costure est muedre (si com dirent li ancien), et c’est ovraiges sens paor;	then treat the wound without stitching or restrictive bandages, for the paper (or dressing) renews itself with the healing of the wound and its gathering, but stitching is moved (as the ancients said), and this causes pain without benefit.
et si a une autre maniere:	and if in another way:
et est que tu seignes la papiere d’une figure qui soit ausi com li fuelle de mirte, si com nos avons conteit, a III oncines desevrez selonc la forme qui est ci:	and it is that you sign the paper with a figure that is similar to the shape of a mirror, as we have described, at three points according to the form that is here:
puis cope ceu qui sormonte as petites forces igalment selonc la forme qui est ci:	Then take those who are weak and equalize their small forces according to this form:
Et se tu n’as pooir de tenir les tenailles, et li chose n’est mie igalz, si prent une aguille ou il ait I fil, et la boute emmi la figure;	And if you cannot hold the pincers steady, and the task is not even, take a needle where there is thread, and wrap it around the object.
et boute I autre fil delez lou grant larmier, et lou secont fil delez lou petit, et assemble entre tes dois les filz igalment;	and wrap another thread around the larger tear, and the second thread around the smaller one, and gather the threads equally between your fingers.
puis lieve ta main igalment, et lieve tout le cuir sus coi tu as signiet, si com nos avons conteit, puis assemble les II levres de la plaie par costure, et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	then gently hold your hand equally, and press all the skin where you have marked it, as we have said, then sew together both edges of the wound, and treat it until it is healed.
et se aposteme vient a ton incision, si l’apaise de cerote et de semblans oignement assouajans;	and if an abscess comes to your incision, calm it with wax and similar remedies that soothe.
et aucune fois avient que li poil de la papiere sont convertit:	and never does it happen that the paper's fibers are changed.
si covient que tu uses ceu que nos avons dit de l’incision;	it is necessary that you use what we have said about the incision;
mais li costure en l’une et en l’autre est plus artificialz.	but stitching on one side and the other is more artificial.
Li cure des caines si est selonc ceste forme:	The treatment of dogs is as follows:
et est que tu convertisses la papiere et la fent dedens selonc ceu que j’ai dit, et puis fai II caines par art, et II liiens subtilz ausi lonc com li papiere et li largesce dou spatumile est;	and it is that you convert the paper and make it inside according to what I have said, and then make two strips with skill, also as long and wide as the paper with a delicate tool.
et cope as II chiés de II pars ou tu tiens les filz;	and cut as well the parts where you hold the threads;
puis assemble l’un et l’autre subtilment sus ceu que sormonte de la papiere de l’oil, et estrain les II cainnes des II parties forment;	then carefully join the two parts together over the paper from the oil, and strain the two strips from the two parts formed.
et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, et li cuir qui iert estrainte morra et nercira et porrira, tant qu’il cherra par lui.	and leave it thus for several days, and the skin that is strained will die and contract and heal, as long as it remains in place.
S’il tarde, si le cope a unes forces, puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	If it's delayed, if the patient has any strength, then treat it while he is healthy;
et quant li plaie iert soudee, et si ert levee li papiere, et ne poindront plus li poil;	and if the wound is deep and fresh, and when it is opened, the papers (scab) are lifted, and the hairs do not grow back.
et c’est li forme des II cainnes que tu feras selonc ceste figure, et selonc ceste quantiteit de lonc et de large:	and this is the shape of the two lines that you will make according to this figure, and according to this length and width.
li ovraiges est telz que tu preignes une aguille subtil, et i boute I fil de soie souef et subtil;	the work involves piercing with a fine needle and threading it with soft and delicate silk thread;
puis assemble les chiés et noe l’un et l’autre subtilment, et soit li longesce des filz une palme de lonc;	then gather the joints and gently join them together, so that the length of the bones is a palm's length.
puis ordene en la chasse I autre fil subtil de soie briément, et noe les chief dou fil;	then arrange in the wound another fine thread of silk briefly, and join the ends delicately with the main thread.
puis mette li malaides son chief en ton sain;	then place the patient's head in a healthy position.
et soit delez lou soleil si que li ovraiges soit declairiez, car c’est uns ovraiges subtilz et menus, puis boute l’aguille a tout la chasse en la racine dou poil ajosteit, et la fai percier en la papiere hastanment tant que tu la traies desus lou poil natureil;	and make the sun shine through so that the work is revealed, for it is a delicate and small task. Then insert the needle throughout the wound at the root of the hair gently, piercing the paper-thin skin until you reach the natural hair below.
puis estrai le poil jusque sus la chasse, et boute en la chasse celui poil, s’il en i a I ou II ou III ou plusors;	then extract the hair right up to the root, and push the hair back into the root if there is one or two or three or more;
puis estrai ta main tant que li poilz veigne fuers a tout la chasse en la papiere avec lou poil natureil.	then extend your hand until the hairs come out completely from the root in the paper with the natural hair.
Et se li chasse est traite et li poilz ne vient fuer avec li, si trairas la chasse au desoz a tout le fil que tu i as ordeneit, tant que li chasse veigne fuer dou pertus desus et que tu la voies par la vision de l’oil;	And if the root is treated and the hair does not come out with it, then pull on the root from inside out until the whole thread that you had ordered comes out, as long as the root comes out completely through the opening above and you see it with the eye's vision.
adonques si trairas la chasse et le fil, et clo l’oil et lou laisse clo II jors ou III, tant que li poil s’aerde en son leu et naisse li char sus;	Then take the hook and thread, and close the wound with oil and leave it for two or three days until the hair grows back in its place and the scar heals.
et se li poilz est petis, si acompaigne I poil lonc des chevoulz naturez, et soit alevez avec celui ou tu le laisse, tant qu’il soit eslongiez et puis le lieve.	and if the hairs are small, accompany them with the long hairs of natural growth, and raise it with that or leave it until it elongates and then remove it.
de la porriture de l’oil	regarding the impurity of oil
Quant ceste maladie qui est apelee «aleacrati» ou li porriture vient en l’oil, si en i a de II manieres:	When this disease called "aleacrati" or putrefaction occurs in the oil, it has two manners:
l’une natureil, et l’autre innatureil.	One naturally, and the other unnaturally.
Et avient par soudement de plaie, ou de tailleure ou de cautere, et par semblans choses.	And it happens suddenly from a wound, or cutting, or cautery, and similar things.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige en li est que tu fendes celle soudure, et dessevre les levres de li, et met dedens tentes de lin, et la lie tant qu’elle soit sanee;	And the method of working on it is that you split that suture, separate the lips, and place cloth inside, binding it until it is healed.
et ne covient mie que tu uses en la cure de li de choses que sechent et restraignent.	and it is not advisable that you use things that dry and constrict in the treatment of it.
Car se tu fais ceu, si revient li maladie pire que li premiere;	For if you do that, the illness will return worse than before;
mais i oevre de choses amollissans, si com fenugreic;	but I work with softening substances, such as fennel.
et l’arose d’aigue ou altee et semence de lin soient cuites, et oignemens dyaquilon fondut en aucun des oiles, et i envoloupe une tente, et le cure de ceu.	and the rosewater of water or linseed, cooked, and the diaquiled onions melted in either oil, and it envelops a bandage, and the treatment of this.
Et li tresors de ta cure si est que tu te dones en garde qu’ele ne soude mie selonc la forme qu’elle fut devant;	And the true treasure of your cure is that you take care not to let it harden according to its former shape.
et cist ovraiges que nos avons dit nen est fuers que adresemens de ceste maladie, qu’elle ne reviegne selonc la forme qu’elle fut devant.	and these works that we have spoken are not only remedies for this illness, but also to prevent it from returning in the same form as before.
de la char qui vient en l’oil	of the grease that comes to the eye
Ceste maladie que est desoz qui vraiement est apelee «axacrati», et est naturelz et accidens.	This illness which is dislocation, truly called "axacrati," is both natural and accidental.
Li accidens vient de plaie et de fendure et de cautere et de choses semblans;	The accident arises from wounds, cuts, cautery, and similar things;
et li voie de l’ovraige en li si est que tu preignes un aguille, en coi il ait I fil double, et la fiche en la char, et li fai percier des le senestre larmier tant c’a destre, si que li filz veigne en II chiés de la char;	and the path to success in it is such that if you press an needle, having a double thread, and insert it into the skin, starting from the left tear (i.e., side), so that the thread comes out on the right side of the skin;
puis estent la char au desus a tout l’aguille, et la cope a I spatumile large.	then the skin is pulled tight over the entire needle, and the flap at the incision site is wide.
Et se li figure de la papiere revient selonc ceu qu’il covient, c’est boin;	And if the shape of the paper returns to what is appropriate, it is good.
se ceu non, si pren I raseur et le met en la fendure, et torne la papiere, et fent II fendures ou costeit dedens la papiere;	If this is not done, take a razor and place it in the split, turn the paper, and make two cuts on either side inside the paper.
et soient li chiés des II fendures des II angles de l’incision que tu as copeit, et soit fais uns angles si que quant elles sont assemblees, que li figure soit ausi com li figure d’une lettre qui a non «I griesche»;	and let the seeds of the two cuts be at the two corners of the incision you have made, and make them form an angle so that when they are joined together, the shape is like the letter 'I Greek'.
puis oste celle char, selonc la quantiteit que ses costez est agus desoz, de ceu qui enseut la papiere, puis ajoste les II parties desevrees, et les cout d’un fil de lainne;	then cut this one, according to the thickness of its edges, from the paper, then adjust the two parts and sew them with a thread of wool.
puis lou cure de ceu que nos avons dit des medicines mollifians, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez.	then apply the treatment of those things we have spoken of regarding soft and gentle medicines, as long as he is healthy.
Et se li maladie vient de fendure ou de costure ou de cautere, si covient que tu fendes une fendure plainne desoz les poilz des papieres, et selonc ceu qui est ci devant;	And if the illness comes from a wound or stitching or cauterization, it is necessary that you make a clean cut beneath the skin and paper-like hairs, following what has been said above.
puis desevre entre les II leivres d’une tente, si com j’ai dit;	then separate between the two parts of a tent, as I have said;
et doit on faire l’ovraige selonc la forme de la maladie, car elle est mout diverse en forme, et li saiges maistres appareille engien de tout som pooir coment il faice revenir la figure a sa forme natureil;	and one must perform the work according to the form of the illness, for it is very diverse in form, and wise masters have devised various means by which they can restore the natural shape.
et li malaides meisme, selonc ceu qu’il i covient d’ovraige et d’estrumens em plusors dispositions.	and instruct the patient himself, according to what is necessary for the operation and using various instruments in different positions.
dou soudement de la papiere	The phrase "dou soudement de la papiere" does not have a clear or straightforward
Quant ceste soudure avient a mains homes en teil maniere que li papiere desus est sodee avec le blanc de l’oil, et ne puet movoir ne faire ses ovraiges naturez, si covient donques que tu i boutes la pointe d’un raseur desoz la papiere, et la lieve en haut;	When this suture is done by untrained hands in such a way that the paper (bandage) on top is smooth with oil and cannot move or perform its natural functions, then you must insert the tip of a razor under the paper and lift it slightly.
et l’estent as pinceures, tant que tu copes ceu qui est aert au spatumile subtil, qui ne soit mie trop agus ne trop trenchans, si que li malaides ne puisse soffrir que li spatumile trop agus ne blecent l’oil;	and stretch it as if using pincers, while you carefully do what is necessary with a very thin spatula, not too sharp or too blunt, so that the patient does not suffer from the overly sharp spatula and it does not cut through the oil.
et soit ton incision, dont tu escorche celle assemblee, legierement, si que li papiere reviegne selonc sa forme natureil;	and let your cut, which you make on the affected part, be light, so that the skin regains its natural shape.
et est sanee toute celle assemblee, et font aucune fois en l’oil aigue salee, et le leve d’aigue douce, et de coliere;	and it becomes healthy, and never form pus in the infected part, nor create an abscess of foul-smelling water, or a swell of clear water, or a collar.
puis met entre la papiere et l’oil une tente de lin, et met sus l’oil laine moillie en abun d’uef;	then place a thin linen cloth between the paper and the oil, and put over the oil a generous amount of damp wool.
et aprés le tier jor use dou coliere et des choses soudans tant qu’il soit sanez.	and after the third day, apply hot compresses and suds until it is healed.
de l’ungle de l’oil	from the nail of the finger
Saiches que li ungle est selonc II manieres:	You know that the nail is according to two manners:
elle est nervouse et semblans a I dur syfac, et une autre qui n’est mie nervouse, mais est semblans a blainche moistor congelee, que quant on la touche de fer et on la cuide panre as pinceures, si ne puet om;	it is nervous and appears hard and dry, and another that is not nervous at all, but appears like white, frozen moisture, which when touched with iron and treated with forceps, cannot be moved by anyone.
et l’une et l’autre semblance encomence devers le grant larmier, et croist poc et poc tant qu’ele cuevre toute la veue et toute la lumiere et le movement de l’oil.	and both appearances begin towards the great lacrimal gland, growing smaller and smaller until they cover all vision and all light and the movements of the eye.
Et li maniere de l’incision si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, puis li oevre les eulz;	And the manner of the incision is that the patient places his head on the healthy side, then opens them (the eyes).
et lieve la papiere a ta main, puis coil l’ungle as pinceures de petite doubleure, et l’estent au desus;	and hold the paper in your hand, then bend the finger like a small pincers, and stretch it above.
puis pren une aguille, et i met I poil de cheval, ou de vaiche, ou de buef, et I fil fort;	then take a needle, and insert a horsehair, or a goose feather, or ox hair, and tie it tightly.
et double la pointe de l’aguille un poc et la fiche emmi l’ungle, et la perce a tout l’aguille, et lie l’ungle d’un fil et l’estent au desus, et escorche a tout lou poil le costeit de l’ungle qui enseut la prunele et la soie au poil jusc’au chief, puis cope lou remanant en la racine dou larmier a tout lou spatumile subtil et as petites forces, et laisse la char natureil ou larmier, si que par l’incision ne veigne li cors des larmes acostumeement;	and double the point of the needle slightly and insert it through the nail, pushing it all the way through the nail bed, and tie the nail with the thread, stretching it above. And scrape along the side of the nail close to the skin using a thin, sharp tool, removing only enough to prevent the nail from splitting or breaking as it grows back naturally, without causing the skin to bleed excessively.
et aucune fois s’estent li ungle a l’oncine soulement, et au fil, si com nos avons dit;	and never extend the nails to the wound only, and with thread, as we have said;
puis l’escorche on a tout le spatumile souef de coi ci est li forme:	then the skin is peeled from the entire soft part, which takes the shape of:
Et garde que li spatumile ne touche la toile charnue et la rompe, et que li prunele ne soit percie;	and ensure that the soft part does not touch the tender flesh and damage it, and that the instrument is not pierced.
et aprés l’incision giete en l’oil un poc de seil broiet, et dou coliere fait de litargire, et le laisse jusc’a l’autre jor;	and after the incision, pour a little of this powder into the wound, and then apply a collar made of litharge, and leave it until the next day;
puis le cure de ceu qu’il i covient tant qu’il soit sanez.	then attend to what is necessary until it is healthy.
Et se li ungle n’est mie nervouse, et tu ne pues bouter l’aguille, et li uncines n’i puet entrer, maintes fois est curee ceste semblance d’ungle de medicines;	And if the nail is not connected to a nerve and you cannot push the needle through it, the hooks cannot enter. Often, this appearance of a nail requires treatment with medicine.
et naissent sicom j’ai conteit en la division, et se tu la vues coper, si oevre l’oil dou malaide, et pren le spatumile legier poc agut selonc ceste forme:	and they grow as I have described in the dissection; and if you see it covering, open gently the wound of the afflicted person, and take a light spatula according to this form.
Et reis l’ungle desus subtilment, et se tu vois qu’elle amenuise point et li rasion i apresse, si distille de ta bouche en l’oil coliere fait de litargire et dou coliere rouge et seil broiet, et estoupe l’oil jusc’a l’autre jor;	And carefully remove the nail from above, and if you see that it becomes softer and the pain subsides, distill this mixture into a collar made of lithargyrum (a type of sulfur) and red dye, and apply the oil to the wound for the next day.
puis rencomence l’autre ovraige selonc ceste meisme oevre, tant qu’elle soit toute ostee.	then begin the other task according to this same work, until it is entirely healed.
Se aucune chose ne t’est contraire en l’oil, si com aposteme chaus, adonques la lait, et cure premier l’aposteme chaut tant qu’il soit sanez, puis rencomence l’ovraige si com devant, tant qu’il soit sanez.	If nothing contradicts you about the oil, such as a hot abscess, then apply it, and treat first the hot abscess until it is healed, and then continue the work as before, until it is completely cured.
Et se li apparance de la chair dou larmier nuit en l’oil par grant nuisement, si la sospent a l’oncine, et en cope une partie et non mie tot, que cors de larmes n’i viegne;	And if the appearance of the flesh from the wound causes great harm in the eye over time, if you suspend it at the point and cut off only a part, not all of it, then the watering (or irritation) will cease.
puis distille en l’oil coliere rouge qui est fais de litargire.	then distill into the eye a red collar made of litharge.
de la char qui naist sus la prunelle	on the flesh that is born on the eyelid
Es eulz d’aucuns homes naist aucune fois char rouge, et cuevre la prunele et restraint sus les papieres et les torne au defuer, et semble une rose de balauste;	Some people's eyes never turn red, and they cover the pupil and rest on papers and turn them into ashes, resembling a rose of balsam.

des voines des eulz	veins of the eyes
Sebel sont voinnes rouges que sont covertes sus l’oil, et tolent a la veue son ovraige et afoiblissent l’oil toz jors.	These are the red veins that are covered over the eye, and they steal from the sight their work and weaken the eye every day.

adonques le coil en teil maniere:	Then tie it in this manner:

de la fistule de l’oil	from the fistula of the oil
Li mire si nomment «arissati» fistule:	They call these "arrested" fistules:
quant tu la cures per cautere et par medicine ague ardant selonc ceu que j’ai devant dit, et elle n’est mie sanee, si est engien en li que tu fendes sus l’aposteme, lai ou il doit meurer, et trai toute la moistor que i est, tant que li os soit descovers.	As you treat it with cautery and medicine for the burning pain as I mentioned earlier, and it does not heal, there is a danger in cutting into the abscess where he must die, and drain all the moisture until the bone is exposed.
Et quant li os iert descovers, et tu verras la corruption et la noiror, si la reis a tout l’estrument de coi ci est li forme;	And when the bone is exposed and you see the corruption and blackness, then take all the instruments mentioned here to shape it.
et est apelez «aspre chief», et soit fait de feir inde a I chief reont, et soit pointoiez si com une lime si com il est en la presente forme:	It is called an "aspire chisel", and it should be made of iron from the root to the tip, and pointed like a limet in the present shape.
Et met sus lou leu de l’os corrumput, puis le torne entre tes dois, et presse ta main un poc tant que tu saiches que celle corruption est rese;	And place the corrupt bone back into its original position, then twist it between your fingers, and press your hand slightly until you know that corruption is healed.
et fai ceu aucune fois, puis restoure lou leu de medicines exiccatives.	and do this once, then return the position with drying medicinal herbs.
se li leus est soudez, et char i naist, et li cors de la bowe est soudez, et remaint ensi XL jors, et il ne renovele et n’est mie apostemez, et accidens mavais n’i vient, saiches qu’il est sanez;	if the bones are fused together, and it grows, and the bowel's opening is fused, and remains like this for forty days, and does not renew or become abscessed, and no bad accidents come, then know that it is healed.

si est plus legiere chose au malaide.	if it is a lighter matter for the patient.
de l’issue de l’oil	from the wound
Quant li eulz apert fuer dou tout en tout, et il ne vient point de destorbier au nef, ne amenuisement, si covient que tu lies lou malaide;	When the joints open widely and cause no disturbance or reduction in respiration, it is necessary to keep the patient still.
puis le saine, puis li met ventouses ou haterel sens ferir por succier, puis met sus l’oil I liien fait d’acaice et de aloe et d’encens et de sarcocolle, et puis estrain l’oil, et l’emplaustre sus de bendes et de drapelz;	then apply health-giving poultices or leeches without causing harm to suck the blood, then place oil made from fennel and aloe and incense and dragon's blood on it, and then strain the oil and apply it over bandages and cloth.

puis oste lou liien aprés le jor et la nut, et se tu vois l’oil repairier, c’est boin;	then remove the bandage after day and night, and if you see that it has healed well, that is good.
se ce non;	If this is not;
si rencomence l’emplaustre et les drapelz et lou liien et les ventouses tant qu’il soit sanez.	If the plaster, bandages, and bindings are re-applied and the suction cups are removed while the wound is healthy.
dou derrompement de toile uvee	loss of fabric integrity
Quant disruptions vient en la toile uvee, puis apert, et vient fuer des papieres si com I grain de resins, et est espoantauble a veoir;	When the wound cloth is removed, it opens up and there comes out something like grains of resin, which is hopeful to see.
adonques se tu la vues coper, li ovraiges est telz que tu boutes une aguille en la racine des la partie desoz jusc’a celi desus, puis boute une autre aguille ou il ait I fil double des la partie dou larmier;	then if you see it covered, the work is such that you pierce a needle into the root of the lower part just above this one, then pierce another needle where there is a double thread from the upper part of the wound.
et la fai percier, et laisse la premiere aguille selonc la disposition;	and pierce it, and leave the first needle according to the arrangement;
puis cope lou leu dou fil double et lie une partie de l’uve entor, et l’estraint bien, puis estrai l’aguille et met sus l’oil lainne moillie en abun d’uef;	then cut the skin with a thread of double thread and tie one part of the eyelid around it, tightening it well, then extract the needle and apply another oil, moistened in abundance;
et le laisse tant que li filz chiece avec l’uve, puis cure l’oil de choses confortans tant que li plaie soit sanee;	and leave it until the thread disintegrates with the eyelid, then apply oil with comforting substances until the wound is healed;
et aucune fois li plaie est restrainte par l’uve chescune part d’un cercle de drap, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	and the wound should never be restrained by the eyelid in any way, as long as it is healed.
Et se li eulz done grant apparance, si le perce au spatumile subtil qui viegne em parfont de l’oil, et corre la moistor albuginé et dessende li eulz, et entre ens tantost;	And if the joint appears to be well-formed, pierce it with a fine instrument that comes from oil, and drive out the white moisture of the joint, and immediately enter within.
puis l’estrai tant qu’il soit sanez.	then extract it as long as it is healthy.
de la bowe de l’oil	from the fat of the oil
Ceste maladie qui est apelee «alcunnati» nen est fuers que bowe qui est assemblee en l’oil, semblant a aigue dessendant, et ce n’est mie aigue;	This illness called "alcunnati" is only characterized by moisture collected in the oil, appearing like sharp descent, but it is not sharp.
et li maniere de l’apparance de l’ovraige si est que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege appareilliet et droit, puis prent le chief entre tes mains de II pars, et lou muef tant que tu voies la bowe venir au desus a tes eulz;	and the manner of the appearance of the work is that you make the patient sit up straight, then take the head in both hands, and move it until you see the moisture rising towards your joints.
puis soit ens fichie, et ne dessende et soit descombree li lumiere, et voie li malaides les choses si com il soloit;	Then it should be firmly fixed, and let no light descend or become dim, and the sick person will see things as they once were.
et s’elle ne dessent desoz, saiches que c’est aigue, et se li dessendemens de la bowe n’est appareilliez si com nos avons dit.	and if the light does not descend, know that it is acute, and if the bowel's descent is not equipped as we have said.
si fai seoir lou malaide entre tes mains, puis prent le spatumile subtil et fent sus la toile cornee I poc par la continuation de la conjunctive avec la toile cornee et la corone, tant que li bowe isse;	if you delay the sick person between your hands, then take the delicate spatula and make incisions on the cornea cloth in the form of a circle along the continuity of the conjunctiva with the cornea and the crown, while the bowel is still present.
et quant elle ert issue, si distille en l’oil aigue chaude mellee a miel, ou aigue ou fenugreic est boillis et miel, puis soit curee d’autre cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	and when it is separated, it should be distilled in hot honey or a mixture of honey and mint, or boiled water with fennel, then treated with another remedy until it is cured.
des aigues de l’oil	The phrase "des aigues de l’oil" translates directly to "of the waters
Nos avons jai les semblances des aigues en la division, et ceu qu’il covient por percier;	We have similar waters in the division, and what is necessary to pierce.
si en oevre selonc la santeit.	if it is done according to health.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains croisiet, fuers de la lumiere por le soleil, et li lie l’oil sain et estreint mout fort;	You should place the patient between your crossed hands away from direct light for the sun, and tie healthy oil firmly to them.
puis met la papiere de l’oil a ta main senestre se li eulz est senestres, ou a ta main destre se li eulz est destres;	then place the paper from oil in your left hand if the joints are on the left, or in your right hand if the joints are on the right.
puis prent en ta main destre, se li eulz est senestres, l’estrument qui est apelez «almagda», ou a ta main senestre, se li eulz est destre;	then, in your right hand if the joints are on the left, take the instrument called "almagda," or in your left hand if the joints are on the right.
puis met la pointe de l’estrument delez la corone par la groissece d’un rait en celle blenchor de l’oil a la partie dou menor larmier, puis boute l’estrument qui est apelez «almagda» vertuousement, et trestorne ta main tant qu’il perce en la blenchor de l’oil, et sente que almagda viegne a la chose vuide;	then, using the tip of the instrument, remove the crust along its thickness from the outermost part towards the inner corner of the eye, then press the instrument called "almagda" gently, and turn your hand until it pierces the membrane of the oil and you feel that "almagda" reaches the empty space.
et covient que li mesure de la voie almagda soit au parfont de la mesure des l’espaice qui est des la prunele jusc’a la fin de la noirour;	and it is necessary that the measure of the magical path be exactly equal to the measure of the space from the tip of the plum to the end of the darkness.
et c’est li corone de l’oil;	and this is the crown of the oil;
si verras l’os en celle papiere por la clarteit de la toile cornee, et pues met l’estrument jusc’a leu ou li aigue est, puis l’espresse desoz une voie aprés autre.	if you will see the bone on this paper due to the clarity of the corny fabric, then place the instrument nearby or where the water is, and then press it from one way to another.
se li aigue dessent maintenant, si voit li malaides devant lui et l’estrument en son oil.	If he lowers himself now, let him see the patient before him and the instrument in his hand.
Aprés repose I petit, et se li aigue remonte la seconde voie, met la fuer avec l’estrument, et quant elle est ens fichie et ele ne monte, si estrai almagda legierement en tornoiant ta main poc et poc;	After resting, let the small one, and then the water climbs up the second way, place the force with the instrument, and when it is firmly stuck and does not rise, gently extract the magical matter by turning your hand back and forth.
et puis remette en aigue un poc de seil gemme, et leive de ceu l’oil dedens.	and then put back in place a little piece of silk string, and remove from these the oil inside.
Puis met par defuer l’oil estoupes ou lainne moillie en oile roset et en abun d’uef, et lie avec l’oil sain.	Then apply hot oil or any other moist oil (roses) and an abundance of heat, and wrap it with healthy oil.
Nos, et cil qui sont de nostre tens, mettons sus comin broiet avec abun d’uef.	We, and those of our time, place a fine, new bandage with abundance of egg.
Et se almagda n’i puet entrer en l’oil par sa duresce, car il i a de teilz homes qui ont trop durs les eulz, si covient que tu preignes l’estrument qui est apelez «alberit», de coi ci est li forme:	And if the foreign body cannot enter the eye due to its hardness, as there are many people with very hard eyelids, it is necessary that you press the instrument called "alberit", which has this shape:
Et perce donques la conjunctive soulement, et n’aler mie trop em parfont, mais fai I leu subtil, puis i boute almagda, si com nos avons dit;	And then pierce only the outer joint, and do not cut too deep, but make it subtle, then apply almagd, as we have said.
et au complissement de l’uevre appareille au malaide I dorteur avenant, en coi il dorme sus son dos en I leu tenebrous;	and upon completion of the work, prepare for the patient a comfortable bed, so that he sleeps on his back in a dark place.
et soit deveez de toz movemens, et preigne legieres viandes, et ne mueve son chief ne a destre ne a senestre, et soit liiez selonc sa disposition jusc’a tier jor;	and he should be restricted from all movements, and given light foods, and not move his head to the right or left, and be bound according to his condition for up to three days.
puis le deslie en cele maison meisme tenebrouse, et esprueve sa veue, et lou fai veoir aucunes choses, et puis li remet lou lien jusc’a septime jor;	then loosen it in the same dark place, test its vision, and make it see nothing, and then put back the bandage until the seventh day.
et ne covient mie que tu faices ceu en l’oure de la cure ou aprés l’incision maintenant, mais il covient que tu aliges ceu, por ceu que li aigue monte hastanment.	and it is not advisable that you do this during the treatment or after the incision now, but rather you should lighten it, because the sharp pain has increased severely.
se apostemes chaus vient, que tu desliies l’oil devant le septime jor, et l’adrece de ceu qui assouaige aposteme;	if abscesses occur, that you loosen the bandage before the seventh day and apply the remedies for the healed abscess.
et quant il est apaisiez, si deslie la veue et met sus sa faice I orilliet por covrir aucun jor, et soit adés en celle maison tenebrouse.	and when it is calmed, loosen the vision and place a side on his face to cover any light, and be in that dark house again.
Et puis isse de la maison poc et poc, et se convertisse en ses cas;	Then he goes out of the house little by little and returns to his usual self.
et saiches que nulz deciples ne se doit entremettre en cest cas.	and knows that no disciple should intervene in this case.
Et uns vint a nos qui estoit de la Yrach, qui nos dist que en som pais faisoit om almagda perciet, a coi on succe l’aigue, mais toutevoie je n’en vis onques nul en nostre terre, ne je ne lou lis onques en livres des anciens;	And one came to us from the East who told us that in their peaceful lands, they made an instrument which sucked out water, but I never saw one in our land, nor do I read about it in the books of the ancients.
et par aventure c’est une novele chose.	and by chance, this is a new thing.
Et ce sont les semblances des formes de almagda, por ceu que cil qui ne les conoit les voie;	And these are the appearances of the shapes of magic, because whoever does not know them will see them differently.
et soient d’arain proprement:	and let them be of gold properly:
Et soient li chief d’aus de ceste meisme subtiliteit, et li derriene en III angles ague.	And let the front of this same subtlety be sharp, and the rear in three acute angles.
de la char sor le neis	Of the pain near the nose
Aucune fois naissent ou neis chars ajostees diverses, de coi il i a aucunes qui semblent scorpions a mout de piez;	No creature ever born or formed with diverse joints will have any that seem like scorpions in their multitude.
et si i a de telz ou il ait char enchancree de fuxe color, et si a char souef de bone color.	and if it has such as it has been charmed with bright colors, and if the hair is soft and of good color.
En celle donques de ces chars qui est souef, et ne mie enchancree, covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains encontre lou soleil;	In this case where the wound is sore and not yet healed, it is necessary that you make the patient rest between your hands facing the sun.
et oevre ses narines, et giete l’oncine a celles chars, et les trai fuers;	and open the patient's nostrils, and pour the liquid into those wounds, and treat them vigorously.
pues cope ceu que tu em pues sostenir au spatumile subtil agut d’une part, tant que tu saiches que celle char est toute ostee.	then hold what you can sustain of the thin, sharp spatula on one side, as long as you know that the wound is entirely opened.
Et s’il en remaint aucune chose c’on ne puisse coper, si l’ovrez a tout I des estrumens subtil legierement, si qu’il n’i demoure rien;	And if there remains anything that cannot be covered, open it completely with all the delicate, light instruments, so that nothing remains.
et se sans te sormonte, ou aposteme chaus, si lou secort si com il covient;	and without stirring or moving, you must clean the abscess as it should be;
et se c’est apostemes malignes, si te haste et lou cauterize tant que li sans soit estainchiez et soient ostees toutes les chars, puis giete ou neis aisil et aigue ou vin.	and if these are malignant abscesses, act swiftly and cauterize them until the pus is drained and all the channels are closed; then apply new, clean, and cool compresses with wine or vinegar.
Se li neis oevre, et moistors en vient jusc’a palais, saiches qu’il est sanez;	If the new wound opens and moisture reaches the palate, knowing it is healthy;
et se moistors ne perce si com il covient, saiches qu’il i a char nee en l’os desus, a coi li estrumens ne vient mie por taillier:	and if the moisture does not open as it should, knowing there is a channel in the bone above, preventing the tools from cutting.
adonques covient il que tu i boutes I fil de lin un poc gros, et soit noez de mains nous, et ait entre chescun nout d’espaice I doit ou moins;	Then you must insert a thread slightly thick, and be careful with your hands, and leave enough space between each one, either more or less.
et mette li malaides lou chiés dou fil en son neif a som pooir, et traie en odorant tant qu’il viegne par lou neif dedens la bouche;	and place the patient's feet with the thread in their armpits, and rub them gently until the thread comes out through the armpit into the mouth.
et maintes fois font ensi li enfant as escoles, et c’est legiere chose a celui qui le vuet faire;	and often children learn this practice, and it is an easy thing for those who wish to do so.
puis tien le chief qui vient par lou neif a une main, et l’autre chief qui vient par la bouche a l’autre main, et saiche l’un aprés l’autre en soiant as nous qui sont ou fil.	then hold the head that comes through the armpit in one hand, and the other head that comes through the mouth in the other hand, and pass them back and forth as we are doing with thread.
Fai ceu tant que tu saiches que li nout ont corrompue celle char, puis trai lou filz, essue le sanc, et moille lou fil en oignement egiptien, et le remet derechief au neis si com devant;	Do as you know, corrupt the new wound, then treat the child, wipe away the blood, and moisten the wound with Egyptian ointment, and then put it back to its place as before.
fai ceu III jors ou plus, tant que li oignemens corrode tout ceu qui est demorez de char;	Do this for three days or more, until the ointment corrodes all that is left from the wound.
et puis met ou neis une caine de plonc aucuns jors tant qu’il soit sanez, et s’il a mestier de medicines sechans, si en use;	and then put a bandage around the neck for no more than days until it is healed, and if it needs dry medicines, use them.
et c’est li forme de l’estrument por purgier lou chief, a coi on distille les oiles et les medicines ou neis:	and this is the form of the instrument to purify the head, from which the oils and medicines are distilled:
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain, semblant a une lampe overte, si com une cainne, et li conduis ausi;	and it should be of silver or gold, resembling an open lamp, like a candlestick, and lead it thither.
et se tu vues, si fai une cainne close, et soit li estrumens plains por espurgier lou chief;	and if you make a closed candlestick, then it is the instrument to purge the head;
et ait I mainche au chief por lou tenir quant on chaufe l’oile ou aucune liquor.	and it should have many parts attached to the head to hold it when heating the oil or any liquid.
de la char sor le neis	Of the pain near the nose
Maintes fois naist au chief dou neis une maladie qui est apelee «telul», et croist et devient grans adés, tant qu’il est vis chose au regarder;	Many times a disease appears on the head due to a condition called "telul," it grows and becomes great over time, as long as it is visible to the eye.
et por ceu covient que tu lou copes au comencement, et l’oste tout fuer, puis met sor leu lou cautere ou la medicine ardant;	and for this reason, it is necessary that you grasp it firmly at the beginning, completely remove it, and then apply the hot cautery or burning medicine.
et s’on le tarde a coper tant qu’il soit grans, si pren warde s’il est durs, de fuxe color, de povre sens:	and if it is not treated quickly while it is still small, take care if it becomes hard, of a dark color, or lacks sensation.
si ne lou touchier mie de fer car c’est uns apostemes enchancrez, car quant on le cope aucune fois, si en vient grant malice au malaide;	do not touch it with iron, as it is an abscess that has grown worse, for when you remove it, great harm comes to the patient.
et se li apostemes est de soef touchement, non mie de fuxe color, et tu vois c’on le puisse tout coper, si vuide le malaide et lou cope sens paor, et cure le leu de choses sechans et restraignans.	and if the abscess is of soft touch, not filled with pus, and you can completely cover it, if the patient allows and treats it without fear, it heals the limb by drying and restraining.
quant li neis est copez et cosus	when the nose is cut and closed
Saiches que quant solutions de continuation vient en une de ces cartillagines ovraiges, i profite poc, fuer que en aucuns homes.	Know that when the continuation of one of these powerful cartilages is broken, it benefits no one.
Il covient donques cant ceu avient a aucun, si regarde se li plaie est fresche a tout son sanc;	One should therefore pay attention so that this does not happen to anyone, if you consider whether the wound is fresh and filled with blood.
et adonques ajoste les II levres a une costure, puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	and then adjust the two edges with a stitch, then treat it until it is healed.
et se les levres sont ja desevrees d’une part et d’autre, si covient que tu escorches toutes les parties de lor keur tant qu’elles sainent, puis assemble les II levres a une costure, et l’estraint, et poudre sus poudre de sanc de dragon, et encens broiet;	and if the lips are loose on both sides, it is necessary that you burn all parts of their edges until they heal, then adjust the two edges with a stitch and tighten them, and apply powdered dragon's blood and incense dust.
et met sus les poudres une piece d’emplaustre de fort ou d’autre emplaustre soudant, et le laisse tant qu’il chiece par lui, puis le cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	and place a piece of plaster, strong or otherwise, over it and leave it until the pain disappears, then apply a healing treatment until it is healed.
Li maniere de la costure si est que tu assembles la solution:	The method of stitching is such that you join the pieces together:
ou par aguilles, si com nos avons dit en la costure dou ventre;	or with needles, as we have said in the stitching of the belly;
ou par fil, si com je le t’ai fait savoir.	or with thread, as I have made known to you.
des apostemes des levres	abscesses of the lips
A mains homes avient dedens les levres aposteme dur, semblans a grains de veces, et menor et plus grant;	At home, there often appear hard abscesses on the lips, resembling small stones, both large and small.
adonques couvient que tu tornes les levres, et fendes sus chescun nout, et le prent as pinceures et le cope en chescune partie;	then you must turn the lips and make a cut on each one, and take them with tweezers and remove them from each part.
puis emple lou leu aprés l’incision de vitriole broiet, tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	then apply the hot (vitriole, a type of sulfuric acid) to the wound until the sight is cleared.
et puis lou leive d’aisil, et cure lou leu de choses seches tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then the cold (air) from the silk, and treat the wound with dry things until it is healed.
de la char des gencives	from the work of the gums
Maintes fois naist sus les gencives char ajostee, que li ancien apelent «albulus»;	Many times a swelling appears on the gums, which the ancients call "albulus".
si covient que tu la sostienes as tenailles, et la cope a sa racine, et laisse corre la bowe ou le sanc;	It is necessary that you hold it with pincers, cut off the root, and let the pus or blood flow out.
puis met sor le leu vitriole broiet, ou autres poudres restraignans et desiccatives;	then place on it vitriol powder, or other powders that constrict and dry up.
et se celle char revient aprés l’incision, et maintes fois avient, si la cope la seconde fois, et la cauterize:	and if it returns after the incision, this happens many times, if the pus comes out a second time, and then cauterize.
si ne revient mie aprés le cautere;	if it does not return after the cautery;
et ce sont les formes des estrumens por coper.	and these are the shapes of the instruments for closing.
des sordens	from disorders
Aucunes fois sont assemblees au chief des dens, dedens la bouche entre les gencives, escorces qui sont laides et aspres;	Never should they be assembled at the root of the teeth, inside the mouth between the gums, those scars that are ugly and rough;
et aucune fois sont li dent noir et citrin et vers, tant que li corruption vient a la gencive, et sont li dent puant;	and never should the tooth be black and yellow and rotten, as long as the corruption comes to the gums, and it smells bad;
si covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains, et ses chiés soit en ton saint, et reis les dens ou les escorces aperent, tant qu’il n’i demore rien;	If you want that you make the patient rest in your hands, and his limbs are at ease in yours, and remove any bones or scabs that are protruding, until nothing remains.
et ensi fai de la noiror et de la verdor, et de la jaunice et des autres taiches, tant qu’elles soient mondees;	and do the same for blackness and greenness, jaundice and other colors, as long as they are fresh.
et s’on oste ceu que i est a la premiere rasion, c’est boin;	and if what is at the root of the problem is removed, it is good.
se ceu non, si rencomence a rere le secont jor et lou tier, tant que tu aies tout reis;	if not, then return to reading the second and third times, until everything is removed.
et saiches que li dent ont mestier de diverses formes d’estrumens por reire, selonc ceu que li oevre lou demoustre, por ceu que li raseur dont on reit defuer les dens ont autres formes que cil dont on reit entre les dens;	and know that the tooth requires different shapes of instruments to remove, according to what the work demonstrates, because the plier used to pull out the teeth has a different shape than that used between the teeth.
et cestes formes et autres soient avec toi appareillies.	and these shapes and others should be prepared with you.
Il covient quant tu cures lou dent de sa dolor que tu tardes dou traire tant com tu pues, car ce ne doit om mie faire;	When treating a tooth causing pain, it is important to take your time and apply gentle pressure as much as possible, for no one should ever use excessive force.
car c’est une substance mout haute jusc’a donc c’on n’ait point d’excusation dou raier.	because it is a very sticky substance, so there should be no excuse for pulling.
Adonques quant li malaides est constrains dou traire, si covient que tu soies certains dou dent doillant.	Then, when the patient is constrained from drawing out the tooth, it is necessary that you be certain about which tooth is painful.
Maintes fois desoit li dolor lou malaide, et cuide qu’elle soit ou dent saint, et fait traire le boin dent;	Many times the patient suffers great pain, and believes it is from a tooth or gum issue, and has the good tooth pulled.
et toutevoie ne se depart mie li dolor per ceu, tant que li malvais estrais, car nos l’avons ja veut faire a ces sainors;	but the pain does not cease for them until the evil is removed, as we have already tried this on our patients.
et quant tu es bien certains dou dent doillant, si covient que tu escorches entor lou dent a tout i. spatumile fort por warder la gencive de toutes pars;	and when you are well certain of the painful tooth, it is necessary that you scrape around the tooth with a strong spatula to remove all the gums from all sides;
puis le mues a tes dois ou as tenailles subtilz au premier poc et poc, tant qu’il soit bien eslochiés, puis i afferme bien les tenailles;	then move it with your fingers or subtle pliers bit by bit, as long as it is well dislocated, then firmly hold the pliers.
et soit li chiés dou malaide en ton saint entre tes genous, et lou tien bien si qu’il ne se mueve.	and place the patient's dislocated joint in your holy hands between the knees, and hold it firmly so that it does not move.
Aprés estrai lou dent droitement sens brisier, et s’il ne saut fuer, si prent aucun de ces estrumens et le boute dedens de chescune part legierement, et lou remuef si com tu as fait premier.	After extracting the tooth correctly without breaking it, if it does not come out, take none of these instruments and press it gently from every side, and move it as you have done before.
Et se li dens est perciez et mengiez, si covient que tu l’emplisses de drapelz, lai ou li pertus sont;	If the bone is broken and fractured, it is necessary to fill the space with cloth, either in the wound or the gap.
et si l’estraint subtilment as tenailles, que il ne brise a l’estraindre;	and if it is tightly grasped with pliers, do not force it so that it does not break.
et covient mout saigement ovrer entor la gencive por deschaucier lou dent.	and it is necessary to carefully cut around the gum to extract the tooth.
Et te done bien en warde que tu ne le brises, et en remaigne une partie, et reveigne au malaide par la malice de la racine plus grans dolors de la premiere.	Take good care so as not to break it, and if a piece remains, return it to the patient; by the evil of its root, he will suffer greater pain than before.
Et te warde que tu ne faices mie ensi com font li ignorant sainor, qui par lor haste et par lor hardiesce brisent aucune fois le charreit, et n’i amenistrent mie ceu que nos avons conteit;	And be wary that you do not act like the ignorant healers who, through their haste and boldness, break the healing process each time, and do not follow what we have described.
mais font venir aucune fois par l’oquison de ceu grant maladie por les racines que i demorent, ou por lou charreit qu’il brisent, si com nos avons sovent veut;	but they bring about this great disease through the moisture that lingers or through the damage they cause to the joints, just as we have often seen.
et quant li dens est trais, si lavez lou leu de vin ou d’aisil et de seil;	and when the swelling is severe, wash the affected area with wine or ash and silk.
et se decorremens de sanc i vient, que sovent avient, si emple lou leu de vitriole broiet;	and the inflammation of blood, which often occurs, can be alleviated by applying the juice of broken glass.
et se ceu ne vaut, si le cauterize.	and if this does not help, then cauterize him.
Les formes des estrumens, a coi om muet les dens premier, soient a longes pointes et a gros mainches, qu’il ne doublent mie quant tu trairas le dent;	The instruments should have long, sharp points and thick handles so that they do not bend when pulling the tooth.
et ce sont les formes:	and these are the shapes:
Et soient de gros membres si qu’il ne ploient mie au traire, et soient de fer inde bien fait, et soient dentez por mues tenir.	And they should be large members so that they do not bend when pulled, and made of iron well-forged, and toothed for proper movement.
de la racine des dens	from the root of the teeth
Quant li racine demoure au traire, si covient que tu mettes sor le leu coton moilliet em burre I jor ou II, tant que li leus soit amolis, pues i boute les tenailles qui sont apelees «algefri», de coi li chiés semblet bec de soigne;	When the root persists during extraction, it is necessary to place a piece of moist cotton or butter on it for one or two days until the tooth becomes loosened. Then, use the pliers called "algefri," which resemble a care-full hook.
et soient dedens faites ausi com une lime et c’est li forme:	and they should be made as smooth as a lime and this is its shape:
Et se les racines ne vuellent issir a tout ces tenailles, si covient que tu descuevre la char tot entor la racine, et i met l’estrument qui est apelez «althali», c’est a savoir palainche, de coi ci est li forme:	And if the roots do not want to come out of these grips, it is necessary that you uncover the flesh all around the root, and place the instrument called "altali," that is, a plier, which has this form:
Et soit fors et gros si qu’il ne brise mie, et se li racine saut par ceu, c’est boin;	and it should be firm and thick so that it does not break, and if the root jumps out, that is good.
se ceu non, si t’aide de toz les estrumens, de coi les formes vienent ci aprés:	if not, with all the instruments, whose forms come as follows:
Et si s’aide on de cest estrument qui ait II rains, de coi ci est li forme:	And if one uses this instrument with two prongs, its form is:
et d’autres ferremens qui sont devant en la rasion des dens, et de cest estrument qui semble unes grans tenailles, dont ci est li forme:	and other instruments that are used in the treatment of teeth, and this tool that resembles large pincers, whose form is as follows:
Et soit cist estrumens fors qu’il ne puisse brisier, et saiches que mout d’estrumens de dens sont;	and this instrument should be strong so that it does not break, and remember that many instruments from within are.
et ausi d’autres estrumens, qui ne sont mie contez;	and also of other instruments, which are not mentioned;
